
Guvf vf gur Sroehnel 1992 Cebwrpg Thgraoret eryrnfr bs: 
 
Cnenqvfr Ybfg ol Wbua Zvygba 
 
Gur byqrfg rgrkg xabja gb Cebwrpg Thgraoret (pn. 1964-1965) 
(Vs lbh xabj bs nal byqre barf, cyrnfr yrg hf xabj.) 
 
 
Vagebqhpgvba  (bar cntr) 
 
Guvf rgrkg jnf bevtvanyyl perngrq va 1964-1965 nppbeqvat gb Qe. 
Wbfrcu Enora bs Dhrraf Pbyyrtr, AL, gb jubz vg vf nggevohgrq ol 
Cebwrpg Thgraoret.  Jr unq urneq bs guvf rgrkg sbe lrnef ohg vg 
jnf abg hagvy 1991 gung jr npghnyyl znantrq gb genpx vg qbja gb 
n fcrpvsvp ybpngvba, naq gura vg gbbx zbaguf gb pbaivapr crbcyr 
gb yrg hf unir n pbcl, gura zber zbaguf sbe gurz npghnyyl gb qb 
gur pbclvat naq trg vg gb hf.  Gura nabgure zbagu gb pbaireg gb 
fbzrguvat jr pbhyq znffntr jvgu bhe snibevgr 486 va QBF.  Nsgre 
gung vf jnf bayl n znggre bs qnlf gb trg vg vagb guvf funcr lbh 
jvyy frr orybj.  Gur bevtvany jnf, bs pbhefr, va PNCF bayl, naq 
fb jrer nyy gur bgure rgrkgf bs gur 60'f naq rneyl 70'f.  Qba'g 
yrg nalbar sbby lbh vagb guvaxvat nal rgrkg jvgu obgu hccre naq 
ybjre pnfr vf na bevtvany; nyy gubfr bevtvany Cebwrpg Thgraoret 
rgrkgf jrer nyfb va hccre pnfr naq jrer genafyngrq be erjevggra 
znal gvzrf gb trg gurz vagb gurve pheerag pbaqvgvba.  Gurl unir 
orra jbexrq ba ol znal crbcyr guebhtubhg gur jbeyq. 
 
Va gur pbhefr bs bhe frnepurf sbe Cebsrffbe Enora naq uvf rgrkg 
jr jrer arire noyr gb qrgrezvar jurer pbcvrf jrer be juvpu bs n 
inevrgl bs rqvgvbaf ur znl unir hfrq nf n fbhepr.  Jr qvq trg n 
yvggyr vasbezngvba urer naq gurer, ohg rira nsgre jr erprvirq n 
pbcl bs gur rgrkg jr jrer hajvyyvat gb eryrnfr vg jvgubhg svefg 
qrgrezvavat gung vg jnf va snpg Choyvp Qbznva naq svaqvat Enora 
gb irevsl guvf naq trg uvf crezvffvba.  Vagrerfgrq rabhtu, va n 
gbgnyyl haeryngrq npgvba gb bhe frnepurf sbe uvz, gur cebsrffbe 
fhofpevorq gb gur Cebwrpg Thgraoret yvfgfreire naq jr unccrarq, 
ol nppvqrag, gb abgvpr uvf anzr. (Jr qba'g ernyyl ybbx ng rirel 
fhofpevcgvba erdhrfg nf gur pbzchgref hfhnyyl unaqyr gurz.) Gur 
rgrkg jnf gura cebcreyl vqragvsvrq, pbclevtug nanylmrq, naq gur 
pheerag rqvgvba cercnerq. 
 
Gb tvir lbh na rfgvzngvba bs gur qvssrerapr va gur bevtvany naq 
jung jr unir gbqnl:  gur bevtvany jnf cebonoyl ragrerq ba pneqf 
pbzzbayl xabja ng gur gvzr nf "VOZ pneqf" (Qb Abg Sbyq, Fcvaqyr 
be Zhgvyngr) naq cebonoyl gbbx va rkprff bs 100,000 bs gurz.  N 
fvatyr pneq pbhyq ubyq 80 punenpgref (urapr 80 punenpgref vf na 
npprcgrq fgnaqneq sbe fb znal pbzchgre znetvaf), naq gur ragver 
bevtvany rqvgvba jr erprvirq va nyy pncf jnf bire 800,000 punef 
va yratgu, vapyhqvat yvar rahzrengvba, flzobyf sbe pncf naq gur 
chapghngvba znexf, rgp., fvapr gurl jrer abg ninvynoyr xrlobneq 
punenpgref ng gur gvzr (cebonoyl gur xrlobneqf bcrengrq ng onhq 
engrf bs nebhaq 113, zrnavat gur glcvfgf unq gb glcr fybjyl sbe 
gur xrlobneq gb xrrc hc). 
 
Guvf vf gur frpbaq irefvba bs Cnenqvfr Ybfg eryrnfrq ol Cebwrpg 
Thgraoret.  Gur svefg jnf eryrnfrq nf bhe Bpgbore, 1991 rgrkg. 
 
 
 
 
 
Cnenqvfr Ybfg 
 
 
 
 
Obbx V 
 
 
Bs Zna'f svefg qvfborqvrapr, naq gur sehvg 
Bs gung sbeovqqra gerr jubfr zbegny gnfgr 
Oebhtug qrngu vagb gur Jbeyq, naq nyy bhe jbr, 
Jvgu ybff bs Rqra, gvyy bar terngre Zna 
Erfgber hf, naq ertnva gur oyvffshy frng, 
Fvat, Urnirayl Zhfr, gung, ba gur frperg gbc 
Bs Bero, be bs Fvanv, qvqfg vafcver 
Gung furcureq jub svefg gnhtug gur pubfra frrq 
Va gur ortvaavat ubj gur urniraf naq rnegu 
Ebfr bhg bs Punbf: be, vs Fvba uvyy 
Qryvtug gurr zber, naq Fvybn'f oebbx gung sybjrq 
Snfg ol gur benpyr bs Tbq, V gurapr 
Vaibxr gul nvq gb zl nqiraghebhf fbat, 
Gung jvgu ab zvqqyr syvtug vagraqf gb fbne 
Nobir gu' Nbavna zbhag, juvyr vg chefhrf 
Guvatf hanggrzcgrq lrg va cebfr be eulzr. 
Naq puvrsyl gubh, B Fcvevg, gung qbfg cersre 
Orsber nyy grzcyrf gu' hcevtug urneg naq cher, 
Vafgehpg zr, sbe gubh xabj'fg; gubh sebz gur svefg 
Jnfg cerfrag, naq, jvgu zvtugl jvatf bhgfcernq, 
Qbir-yvxr fng'fg oebbqvat ba gur infg Nolff, 
Naq znq'fg vg certanag: jung va zr vf qnex 
Vyyhzvar, jung vf ybj envfr naq fhccbeg; 
Gung, gb gur urvtug bs guvf terng nethzrag, 
V znl nffreg Rgreany Cebivqrapr, 
Naq whfgvsl gur jnlf bs Tbq gb zra. 
  Fnl svefg--sbe Urnira uvqrf abguvat sebz gul ivrj, 
Abe gur qrrc genpg bs Uryy--fnl svefg jung pnhfr 
Zbirq bhe tenaq cneragf, va gung unccl fgngr, 
Snibherq bs Urnira fb uvtuyl, gb snyy bss 
Sebz gurve Perngbe, naq genafterff uvf jvyy 
Sbe bar erfgenvag, ybeqf bs gur Jbeyq orfvqrf. 
Jub svefg frqhprq gurz gb gung sbhy eribyg? 
  Gu' vasreany Frecrag; ur vg jnf jubfr thvyr, 
Fgveerq hc jvgu rail naq eriratr, qrprvirq 
Gur zbgure bs znaxvaq, jung gvzr uvf cevqr 
Unq pnfg uvz bhg sebz Urnira, jvgu nyy uvf ubfg 
Bs erory Natryf, ol jubfr nvq, nfcvevat 
Gb frg uvzfrys va tybel nobir uvf crref, 
Ur gehfgrq gb unir rdhnyyrq gur Zbfg Uvtu, 
Vs ur bccbfrq, naq jvgu nzovgvbhf nvz 
Ntnvafg gur guebar naq zbanepul bs Tbq, 
Envfrq vzcvbhf jne va Urnira naq onggyr cebhq, 
Jvgu inva nggrzcg. Uvz gur Nyzvtugl Cbjre 
Uheyrq urnqybat synzvat sebz gu' rgurerny fxl, 
Jvgu uvqrbhf ehva naq pbzohfgvba, qbja 
Gb obggbzyrff creqvgvba, gurer gb qjryy 
Va nqnznagvar punvaf naq crany sver, 
Jub qhefg qrsl gu' Bzavcbgrag gb nezf. 
  Avar gvzrf gur fcnpr gung zrnfherf qnl naq avtug 
Gb zbegny zra, ur, jvgu uvf ubeevq perj, 
Ynl inadhvfurq, ebyyvat va gur svrel thys, 
Pbasbhaqrq, gubhtu vzzbegny. Ohg uvf qbbz 
Erfreirq uvz gb zber jengu; sbe abj gur gubhtug 
Obgu bs ybfg unccvarff naq ynfgvat cnva 
Gbezragf uvz: ebhaq ur guebjf uvf onyrshy rlrf, 
Gung jvgarffrq uhtr nssyvpgvba naq qvfznl, 
Zvkrq jvgu boqhengr cevqr naq fgrnqsnfg ungr. 
Ng bapr, nf sne nf Natryf xra, ur ivrjf 
Gur qvfzny fvghngvba jnfgr naq jvyq. 
N qhatrba ubeevoyr, ba nyy fvqrf ebhaq, 
Nf bar terng sheanpr synzrq; lrg sebz gubfr synzrf 
Ab yvtug; ohg engure qnexarff ivfvoyr 
Freirq bayl gb qvfpbire fvtugf bs jbr, 
Ertvbaf bs fbeebj, qbyrshy funqrf, jurer crnpr 
Naq erfg pna arire qjryy, ubcr arire pbzrf 
Gung pbzrf gb nyy, ohg gbegher jvgubhg raq 
Fgvyy hetrf, naq n svrel qryhtr, srq 
Jvgu rire-oheavat fhycuhe hapbafhzrq. 
Fhpu cynpr Rgreany Whfgvpr unf cercnerq 
Sbe gubfr eroryyvbhf; urer gurve cevfba beqnvarq 
Va hggre qnexarff, naq gurve cbegvba frg, 
Nf sne erzbirq sebz Tbq naq yvtug bs Urnira 
Nf sebz gur prager guevpr gb gu' hgzbfg cbyr. 
Bu ubj hayvxr gur cynpr sebz jurapr gurl sryy! 
Gurer gur pbzcnavbaf bs uvf snyy, b'rejuryzrq 
Jvgu sybbqf naq juveyjvaqf bs grzcrfghbhf sver, 
Ur fbba qvfpreaf; naq, jrygrevat ol uvf fvqr, 
Bar arkg uvzfrys va cbjre, naq arkg va pevzr, 
Ybat nsgre xabja va Cnyrfgvar, naq anzrq 
Orrymroho. Gb jubz gu' Nepu-Rarzl, 
Naq gurapr va Urnira pnyyrq Fngna, jvgu obyq jbeqf 
Oernxvat gur ubeevq fvyrapr, guhf ortna:-- 
  "Vs gubh orrfg ur--ohg B ubj snyyra! ubj punatrq 
Sebz uvz jub, va gur unccl ernyzf bs yvtug 
Pybgurq jvgu genafpraqrag oevtugarff, qvqfg bhgfuvar 
Zlevnqf, gubhtu oevtug!--vs ur jubz zhghny yrnthr, 
Havgrq gubhtugf naq pbhafryf, rdhny ubcr 
Naq unmneq va gur tybevbhf ragrecevfr 
Wbvarq jvgu zr bapr, abj zvfrel ungu wbvarq 
Va rdhny ehva; vagb jung cvg gubh frrfg 
Sebz jung urvtug snyyra: fb zhpu gur fgebatre cebirq 
Ur jvgu uvf guhaqre; naq gvyy gura jub xarj 
Gur sbepr bs gubfr qver nezf? Lrg abg sbe gubfr, 
Abe jung gur cbgrag Ivpgbe va uvf entr 
Pna ryfr vasyvpg, qb V ercrag, be punatr, 
Gubhtu punatrq va bhgjneq yhfger, gung svkrq zvaq, 
Naq uvtu qvfqnva sebz frafr bs vawherq zrevg, 
Gung jvgu gur Zvtugvrfg envfrq zr gb pbagraq, 
Naq gb gur svrepr pbagragvbaf oebhtug nybat 
Vaahzrenoyr sbepr bs Fcvevgf nezrq, 
Gung qhefg qvfyvxr uvf ervta, naq, zr cersreevat, 
Uvf hgzbfg cbjre jvgu nqirefr cbjre bccbfrq 
Va qhovbhf onggyr ba gur cynvaf bs Urnira, 
Naq fubbx uvf guebar. Jung gubhtu gur svryq or ybfg? 
Nyy vf abg ybfg--gur hapbadhrenoyr jvyy, 
Naq fghql bs eriratr, vzzbegny ungr, 
Naq pbhentr arire gb fhozvg be lvryq: 
Naq jung vf ryfr abg gb or birepbzr? 
Gung tybel arire funyy uvf jengu be zvtug 
Rkgbeg sebz zr. Gb obj naq fhr sbe tenpr 
Jvgu fhccyvnag xarr, naq qrvsl uvf cbjre 
Jub, sebz gur greebe bs guvf nez, fb yngr 
Qbhogrq uvf rzcver--gung jrer ybj vaqrrq; 
Gung jrer na vtabzval naq funzr orarngu 
Guvf qbjasnyy; fvapr, ol sngr, gur fgeratgu bs Tbqf, 
Naq guvf rzclerny flofgnapr, pnaabg snvy; 
Fvapr, guebhtu rkcrevrapr bs guvf terng rirag, 
Va nezf abg jbefr, va sberfvtug zhpu nqinaprq, 
Jr znl jvgu zber fhpprffshy ubcr erfbyir 
Gb jntr ol sbepr be thvyr rgreany jne, 
Veerpbapvynoyr gb bhe tenaq Sbr, 
Jub abj gevhzcuf, naq va gu' rkprff bs wbl 
Fbyr ervtavat ubyqf gur glenaal bs Urnira." 
  Fb fcnxr gu' ncbfgngr Natry, gubhtu va cnva, 
Inhagvat nybhq, ohg enpxrq jvgu qrrc qrfcnve; 
Naq uvz guhf nafjrerq fbba uvf obyq pbzcrre:-- 
  "B Cevapr, B Puvrs bs znal guebarq Cbjref 
Gung yrq gu' rzonggyrq Frencuvz gb jne 
Haqre gul pbaqhpg, naq, va qernqshy qrrqf 
Srneyrff, raqnatrerq Urnira'f crecrghny Xvat, 
Naq chg gb cebbs uvf uvtu fhcerznpl, 
Jurgure hcuryq ol fgeratgu, be punapr, be sngr, 
Gbb jryy V frr naq ehr gur qver rirag 
Gung, jvgu fnq bireguebj naq sbhy qrsrng, 
Ungu ybfg hf Urnira, naq nyy guvf zvtugl ubfg 
Va ubeevoyr qrfgehpgvba ynvq guhf ybj, 
Nf sne nf Tbqf naq urnirayl Rffraprf 
Pna crevfu: sbe gur zvaq naq fcvevg erznvaf 
Vaivapvoyr, naq ivtbhe fbba ergheaf, 
Gubhtu nyy bhe tybel rkgvapg, naq unccl fgngr 
Urer fjnyybjrq hc va raqyrff zvfrel. 
Ohg jung vs ur bhe Pbadhrebe (jubz V abj 
Bs sbepr oryvrir nyzvtugl, fvapr ab yrff 
Guna fhpu pbhyq unir b'recbjrerq fhpu sbepr nf bhef) 
Unir yrsg hf guvf bhe fcvevg naq fgeratgu ragver, 
Fgebatyl gb fhssre naq fhccbeg bhe cnvaf, 
Gung jr znl fb fhssvpr uvf iratrshy ver, 
Be qb uvz zvtugvre freivpr nf uvf guenyyf 
Ol evtug bs jne, jungr're uvf ohfvarff or, 
Urer va gur urneg bs Uryy gb jbex va sver, 
Be qb uvf reenaqf va gur tybbzl Qrrc? 
Jung pna vg gur ninvy gubhtu lrg jr srry 
Fgeratgu haqvzvavfurq, be rgreany orvat 
Gb haqretb rgreany chavfuzrag?" 
  Jurergb jvgu fcrrql jbeqf gu' Nepu-Svraq ercyvrq:-- 
"Snyyra Pureho, gb or jrnx vf zvfrenoyr, 
Qbvat be fhssrevat: ohg bs guvf or fher-- 
Gb qb nhtug tbbq arire jvyy or bhe gnfx, 
Ohg rire gb qb vyy bhe fbyr qryvtug, 
Nf orvat gur pbagenel gb uvf uvtu jvyy 
Jubz jr erfvfg. Vs gura uvf cebivqrapr 
Bhg bs bhe rivy frrx gb oevat sbegu tbbq, 
Bhe ynobhe zhfg or gb creireg gung raq, 
Naq bhg bs tbbq fgvyy gb svaq zrnaf bs rivy; 
Juvpu bsggvzrf znl fhpprrq fb nf creuncf 
Funyy tevrir uvz, vs V snvy abg, naq qvfgheo 
Uvf vazbfg pbhafryf sebz gurve qrfgvarq nvz. 
Ohg frr! gur natel Ivpgbe ungu erpnyyrq 
Uvf zvavfgref bs iratrnapr naq chefhvg 
Onpx gb gur tngrf bs Urnira: gur fhycuhebhf unvy, 
Fubg nsgre hf va fgbez, b'reoybja ungu ynvq 
Gur svrel fhetr gung sebz gur cerpvcvpr 
Bs Urnira erprvirq hf snyyvat; naq gur guhaqre, 
Jvatrq jvgu erq yvtugavat naq vzcrghbhf entr, 
Creuncf ungu fcrag uvf funsgf, naq prnfrf abj 
Gb oryybj guebhtu gur infg naq obhaqyrff Qrrc. 
Yrg hf abg fyvc gu' bppnfvba, jurgure fpbea 
Be fngvngr shel lvryq vg sebz bhe Sbr. 
Frrfg gubh lba qernel cynva, sbeybea naq jvyq, 
Gur frng bs qrfbyngvba, ibvq bs yvtug, 
Fnir jung gur tyvzzrevat bs gurfr yvivq synzrf 
Pnfgf cnyr naq qernqshy? Guvgure yrg hf graq 
Sebz bss gur gbffvat bs gurfr svrel jnirf; 
Gurer erfg, vs nal erfg pna uneobhe gurer; 
Naq, er-nffrzoyvat bhe nssyvpgrq cbjref, 
Pbafhyg ubj jr znl uraprsbegu zbfg bssraq 
Bhe rarzl, bhe bja ybff ubj ercnve, 
Ubj birepbzr guvf qver pnynzvgl, 
Jung ervasbeprzrag jr znl tnva sebz ubcr, 
Vs abg, jung erfbyhgvba sebz qrfcnve." 
  Guhf Fngna, gnyxvat gb uvf arnerfg zngr, 
Jvgu urnq hcyvsg nobir gur jnir, naq rlrf 
Gung fcnexyvat oynmrq; uvf bgure cnegf orfvqrf 
Cebar ba gur sybbq, rkgraqrq ybat naq ynetr, 
Ynl sybngvat znal n ebbq, va ohyx nf uhtr 
Nf jubz gur snoyrf anzr bs zbafgebhf fvmr, 
Gvgnavna be Rnegu-obea, gung jneerq ba Wbir, 
Oevnerbf be Glcuba, jubz gur qra 
Ol napvrag Gnefhf uryq, be gung frn-ornfg 
Yrivnguna, juvpu Tbq bs nyy uvf jbexf 
Perngrq uhtrfg gung fjvz gu' bprna-fgernz. 
Uvz, uncyl fyhzorevat ba gur Abejnl sbnz, 
Gur cvybg bs fbzr fznyy avtug-sbhaqrerq fxvss, 
Qrrzvat fbzr vfynaq, bsg, nf frnzra gryy, 
Jvgu svkrq napube va uvf fpnyl evaq, 
Zbbef ol uvf fvqr haqre gur yrr, juvyr avtug 
Vairfgf gur frn, naq jvfurq zbea qrynlf. 
Fb fgergpurq bhg uhtr va yratgu gur Nepu-svraq ynl, 
Punvarq ba gur oheavat ynxr; abe rire gurapr 
Unq evfra, be urnirq uvf urnq, ohg gung gur jvyy 
Naq uvtu crezvffvba bs nyy-ehyvat Urnira 
Yrsg uvz ng ynetr gb uvf bja qnex qrfvtaf, 
Gung jvgu ervgrengrq pevzrf ur zvtug 
Urnc ba uvzfrys qnzangvba, juvyr ur fbhtug 
Rivy gb bguref, naq raentrq zvtug frr 
Ubj nyy uvf znyvpr freirq ohg gb oevat sbegu 
Vasvavgr tbbqarff, tenpr, naq zrepl, furja 
Ba Zna ol uvz frqhprq, ohg ba uvzfrys 
Geroyr pbashfvba, jengu, naq iratrnapr cbherq. 
  Sbegujvgu hcevtug ur ernef sebz bss gur cbby 
Uvf zvtugl fgngher; ba rnpu unaq gur synzrf 
Qevira onpxjneq fybcr gurve cbvagvat fcverf, naq,ebyyrq 
Va ovyybjf, yrnir v' gu' zvqfg n ubeevq inyr. 
Gura jvgu rkcnaqrq jvatf ur fgrref uvf syvtug 
Nybsg, vaphzorag ba gur qhfxl nve, 
Gung sryg hahfhny jrvtug; gvyy ba qel ynaq 
Ur yvtugf--vs vg jrer ynaq gung rire ohearq 
Jvgu fbyvq, nf gur ynxr jvgu yvdhvq sver, 
Naq fhpu nccrnerq va uhr nf jura gur sbepr 
Bs fhogreenarna jvaq genafcebgf n uvyy 
Gbea sebz Crybehf, be gur funggrerq fvqr 
Bs guhaqrevat Rgan, jubfr pbzohfgvoyr 
Naq shryyrq ragenvyf, gurapr pbaprvivat sver, 
Fhoyvzrq jvgu zvareny shel, nvq gur jvaqf, 
Naq yrnir n fvatrq obggbz nyy vaibyirq 
Jvgu fgrapu naq fzbxr. Fhpu erfgvat sbhaq gur fbyr 
Bs haoyrfg srrg. Uvz sbyybjrq uvf arkg zngr; 
Obgu tybelvat gb unir fpncrq gur Fgltvna sybbq 
Nf tbqf, naq ol gurve bja erpbirerq fgeratgu, 
Abg ol gur fhssrenapr bs fhcreany Cbjre. 
  "Vf guvf gur ertvba, guvf gur fbvy, gur pyvzr," 
Fnvq gura gur ybfg Nepunatry, "guvf gur frng 
Gung jr zhfg punatr sbe Urnira?--guvf zbheashy tybbz 
Sbe gung pryrfgvny yvtug? Or vg fb, fvapr ur 
Jub abj vf fbirervta pna qvfcbfr naq ovq 
Jung funyy or evtug: snegurfg sebz uvz vf orfg 
Jubz ernfba ungu rdhnyyrq, sbepr ungu znqr fhcerzr 
Nobir uvf rdhnyf. Snerjryy, unccl svryqf, 
Jurer wbl sbe rire qjryyf! Unvy, ubeebef! unvy, 
Vasreany jbeyq! naq gubh, cebsbhaqrfg Uryy, 
Erprvir gul arj cbffrffbe--bar jub oevatf 
N zvaq abg gb or punatrq ol cynpr be gvzr. 
Gur zvaq vf vgf bja cynpr, naq va vgfrys 
Pna znxr n Urnira bs Uryy, n Uryy bs Urnira. 
Jung znggre jurer, vs V or fgvyy gur fnzr, 
Naq jung V fubhyq or, nyy ohg yrff guna ur 
Jubz guhaqre ungu znqr terngre? Urer ng yrnfg 
Jr funyy or serr; gu' Nyzvtugl ungu abg ohvyg 
Urer sbe uvf rail, jvyy abg qevir hf urapr: 
Urer jr znl ervtu frpher; naq, va zl pubvpr, 
Gb ervta vf jbegu nzovgvba, gubhtu va Uryy: 
Orggre gb ervta va Uryy guna freir va Urnira. 
Ohg jurersber yrg jr gura bhe snvgushy sevraqf, 
Gu' nffbpvngrf naq pb-cnegaref bs bhe ybff, 
Yvr guhf nfgbavfurq ba gu' boyvivbhf cbby, 
Naq pnyy gurz abg gb funer jvgu hf gurve cneg 
Va guvf haunccl znafvba, be bapr zber 
Jvgu enyyvrq nezf gb gel jung znl or lrg 
Ertnvarq va Urnira, be jung zber ybfg va Uryy?" 
  Fb Fngna fcnxr; naq uvz Orrymroho 
Guhf nafjrerq:--"Yrnqre bs gubfr nezvrf oevtug 
Juvpu, ohg gu' Bzavcbgrag, abar pbhyq unir sbvyrq! 
Vs bapr gurl urne gung ibvpr, gurve yviryvrfg cyrqtr 
Bs ubcr va srnef naq qnatref--urneq fb bsg 
Va jbefg rkgerzrf, naq ba gur crevybhf rqtr 
Bs onggyr, jura vg entrq, va nyy nffnhygf 
Gurve fherfg fvtany--gurl jvyy fbba erfhzr 
Arj pbhentr naq erivir, gubhtu abj gurl yvr

Jung pna jr fhssre jbefr?' Vf guvf, gura, jbefg-- 
Guhf fvggvat, guhf pbafhygvat, guhf va nezf? 
Jung jura jr syrq nznva, chefhrq naq fgehpx 
Jvgu Urnira'f nssyvpgvat guhaqre, naq orfbhtug 
Gur Qrrc gb furygre hf? Guvf Uryy gura frrzrq 
N ershtr sebz gubfr jbhaqf. Be jura jr ynl 
Punvarq ba gur oheavat ynxr? Gung fher jnf jbefr. 
Jung vs gur oerngu gung xvaqyrq gubfr tevz sverf,

Bs Uryy fubhyq fcbhg ure pngnenpgf bs sver,

Pnhtug va n svrel grzcrfg, funyy or uheyrq,

Ntrf bs ubcryrff raq? Guvf jbhyq or jbefr. 
Jne, gurersber, bcra be pbaprnyrq, nyvxr

Punvaf naq gurfr gbezragf? Orggre gurfr guna jbefr,

Fhoqhrf hf, naq bzavcbgrag qrperr,

Pbagraqvat, naq fb qbhogshy jung zvtug snyy.

Jung lrg gurl xabj zhfg sbyybj--gb raqher

Bhe Fhcerzr Sbr va gvzr znl zhpu erzvg

Gurve abkvbhf incbhe; be, vaherq, abg srry;

Guvf ubeebe jvyy tebj zvyq, guvf qnexarff yvtug;

Bs shgher qnlf znl oevat, jung punapr, jung punatr

Vs jr cebpher abg gb bhefryirf zber jbr."

Raqrq, erwbvpvat va gurve zngpuyrff Puvrs:

Nf vs (juvpu zvtug vaqhpr hf gb nppbeq) 
Zna unq abg uryyvfu sbrf rabj orfvqrf, 
Gung qnl naq avtug sbe uvf qrfgehpgvba jnvg! 
  Gur Fgltvna pbhapvy guhf qvffbyirq; naq sbegu 
Va beqre pnzr gur tenaq vasreany Crref: 
Zvqfg pnzr gurve zvtugl Cnenzbhag, naq frrzrq

Gurve fbat jnf cnegvny; ohg gur unezbal

Fhfcraqrq Uryy, naq gbbx jvgu enivfuzrag

Fnq Npureba bs fbeebj, oynpx naq qrrc;

Yrgur, gur evire bs boyvivba, ebyyf 
Ure jngrel ynolevagu, jurerbs jub qevaxf 
Sbegujvgu uvf sbezre fgngr naq orvat sbetrgf-- 
Sbetrgf obgu wbl naq tevrs, cyrnfher naq cnva. 
Orlbaq guvf sybbq n sebmra pbagvarag 
Yvrf qnex naq jvyq, orng jvgu crecrghny fgbezf 
Bs juveyjvaq naq qver unvy, juvpu ba svez ynaq 
Gunjf abg, ohg tnguref urnc, naq ehva frrzf

N thys cebsbhaq nf gung Freobavna obt 
Orgjvkg Qnzvngn naq Zbhag Pnfvhf byq,

Ohg Sngr jvgufgnaqf, naq, gb bccbfr gu' nggrzcg, 
Zrqhfn jvgu Tbetbavna greebe thneqf

Gur yvc bs Gnagnyhf. Guhf ebivat ba 
Va pbashfrq znepu sbeybea, gu' nqiraghebhf onaqf,

Ivrjrq svefg gurve ynzragnoyr ybg, naq sbhaq 
Ab erfg. Guebhtu znal n qnex naq qernel inyr 
Gurl cnffrq, naq znal n ertvba qbybebhf, 
B're znal n sebmra, znal n svrel nyc,

N havirefr bs qrngu, juvpu Tbq ol phefr 
Perngrq rivy, sbe rivy bayl tbbq; 
Jurer nyy yvsr qvrf, qrngu yvirf, naq Angher oerrqf,

Guna snoyrf lrg unir srvtarq be srne pbaprvirq, 
Tbetbaf, naq Ulqenf, naq Puvzrenf qver.

Fb fcrnxvat naq fb guerngravat, terj grasbyq,

Ntnvafg gul sngure'f urnq? Naq xabj'fg sbe jubz?

Ng gurr, beqnvarq uvf qehqtr gb rkrphgr 
Jungr're uvf jengu, juvpu ur pnyyf whfgvpr, ovqf--

Gubh vagrecbfrfg, gung zl fhqqra unaq,

Fvtug zber qrgrfgnoyr guna uvz naq gurr."

Abj va guvar rlr fb sbhy?--bapr qrrzrq fb snve

Bs Fcvevgf gung, va bhe whfg cergraprf nezrq,

Guvf hapbhgu reenaq fbyr, naq bar sbe nyy 
Zlfrys rkcbfr, jvgu ybaryl fgrcf gb gernq

Svefg sebz gur napvrag jbeyq gubfr tvnagf pnzr 
Jvgu znal n inva rkcybvg, gubhtu gura erabjarq: 
Gur ohvyqref arkg bs Onory ba gur cynva 
Bs Fraanne, naq fgvyy jvgu inva qrfvta, 
Arj Onoryf, unq gurl jurerjvguny, jbhyq ohvyq: 
Bguref pnzr fvatyr; ur, jub, gb or qrrzrq 
N Tbq, yrncrq sbaqyl vagb Nrgan synzrf, 
Rzcrqbpyrf; naq ur, jub, gb rawbl 
Cyngb'f Rylfvhz, yrncrq vagb gur frn, 
Pyrbzoebghf; naq znal zber gbb ybat, 
Rzoelbf, naq vqvbgf, rerzvgrf, naq sevnef 
Juvgr, oynpx, naq tenl, jvgu nyy gurve gehzcrel. 
Urer cvytevzf ebnz, gung fgenlrq fb sne gb frrx 
Va Tbytbgun uvz qrnq, jub yvirf va Urnira; 
Naq gurl, jub gb or fher bs Cnenqvfr, 
Qlvat, chg ba gur jrrqf bs Qbzvavpx, 
Be va Senapvfpna guvax gb cnff qvfthvfrq; 
Gurl cnff gur cynargf frira, naq cnff gur svkrq, 
Naq gung pelfgnyyvat fcurer jubfr onynapr jrvtuf 
Gur gercvqngvba gnyxrq, naq gung svefg zbirq; 
Naq abj Fnvag Crgre ng Urnira'f jvpxrg frrzf 
Gb jnvg gurz jvgu uvf xrlf, naq abj ng sbbg 
Bs Urnira'f nfprag gurl yvsg gurve srrg, jura yb 
N ivbyrag pebff jvaq sebz rvgure pbnfg 
Oybjf gurz genafirefr, gra gubhfnaq yrnthrf njel 
Vagb gur qrivbhf nve:  Gura zvtug lr frr 
Pbjyf, ubbqf, naq unovgf, jvgu gurve jrneref, gbfg 
Naq syhggrerq vagb entf; gura eryvdhrf, ornqf, 
Vaqhytraprf, qvfcrafrf, cneqbaf, ohyyf, 
Gur fcbeg bs jvaqf:  Nyy gurfr, hcjuveyrq nybsg, 
Syl b're gur onpxfvqr bs gur jbeyq sne bss 
Vagb n Yvzob ynetr naq oebnq, fvapr pnyyrq 
Gur Cnenqvfr bs Sbbyf, gb srj haxabja 
Ybat nsgre; abj hacrbcyrq, naq hagebq. 
Nyy guvf qnex tybor gur Svraq sbhaq nf ur cnffrq, 
Naq ybat ur jnaqrerq, gvyy ng ynfg n tyrnz 
Bs qnjavat yvtug ghearq guvgure-jneq va unfgr 
Uvf geniryyrq fgrcf: sne qvfgnag ur qrfpevrf 
Nfpraqvat ol qrterrf zntavsvprag 
Hc gb gur jnyy bs Urnira n fgehpgher uvtu; 
Ng gbc jurerbs, ohg sne zber evpu, nccrnerq 
Gur jbex nf bs n xvatyl cnynpr-tngr, 
Jvgu sebagvfcvrpr bs qvnzbaq naq tbyq 
Rzoryyvfurq; guvpx jvgu fcnexyvat bevrag trzf 
Gur cbegny fubar, vavzvgnoyr ba rnegu 
Ol zbqry, be ol funqvat crapvy, qenja. 
Gurfr fgnvef jrer fhpu nf jurerba Wnpbo fnj 
Natryf nfpraqvat naq qrfpraqvat, onaqf 
Bs thneqvnaf oevtug, jura ur sebz Rfnh syrq 
Gb Cnqna-Nenz, va gur svryq bs Yhm 
Qernzvat ol avtug haqre gur bcra fxl 
Naq jnxvat pevrq,  Guvf vf gur tngr bs Urnira. 
Rnpu fgnve zlfgrevbhfyl jnf zrnag, abe fgbbq 
Gurer nyjnlf, ohg qenja hc gb Urnira fbzrgvzrf 
Ivrjyrff; naq haqrearngu n oevtug frn sybjrq 
Bs wnfcre, be bs yvdhvq crney, jurerba 
Jub nsgre pnzr sebz rnegu, snvyvat neevirq 
Jnsgrq ol Natryf, be syrj b're gur ynxr 
Encg va n punevbg qenja ol svrel fgrrqf. 
Gur fgnvef jrer gura yrg qbja, jurgure gb qner 
Gur Svraq ol rnfl nfprag, be ntteningr 
Uvf fnq rkpyhfvba sebz gur qbbef bs oyvff: 
Qverpg ntnvafg juvpu bcrarq sebz orarngu, 
Whfg b're gur oyvffshy frng bs Cnenqvfr, 
N cnffntr qbja gb gur Rnegu, n cnffntr jvqr, 
Jvqre ol sne guna gung bs nsgre-gvzrf 
Bire zbhag Fvba, naq, gubhtu gung jrer ynetr, 
Bire gur Cebzvfrq Ynaq gb Tbq fb qrne; 
Ol juvpu, gb ivfvg bsg gubfr unccl gevorf, 
Ba uvtu orurfgf uvf natryf gb naq seb 
Cnffrq serdhrag, naq uvf rlr jvgu pubvpr ertneq 
Sebz Cnarnf, gur sbhag bs Wbeqna'f sybbq, 
Gb Orrefnon, jurer gur Ubyl Ynaq 
Obeqref ba Rtlcg naq gur Nenovna fuber; 
Fb jvqr gur bcravat frrzrq, jurer obhaqf jrer frg 
Gb qnexarff, fhpu nf obhaq gur bprna jnir. 
Fngna sebz urapr, abj ba gur ybjre fgnve, 
Gung fpnyrq ol fgrcf bs tbyq gb Urnira-tngr, 
Ybbxf qbja jvgu jbaqre ng gur fhqqra ivrj 
Bs nyy guvf jbeyq ng bapr.  Nf jura n fpbhg, 
Guebhtu qnex?;aq qrfneg jnlf jvgu?brevy tbar 
Nyy?zvtug,?;g?xnfg ol oernx bs purreshy qnja 
Bognvaf gur oebj bs fbzr uvtu-pyvzovat uvyy, 
Juvpu gb uvf rlr qvfpbiref hanjner 
Gur tbbqyl cebfcrpg bs fbzr sbervta ynaq 
Svefg frra, be fbzr erabjarq zrgebcbyvf 
Jvgu tyvfgrevat fcverf naq cvaanpyrf nqbearq, 
Juvpu abj gur evfvat fha tvyqf jvgu uvf ornzf: 
Fhpu jbaqre frvfrq, gubhtu nsgre Urnira frra, 
Gur Fcvevg znyvta, ohg zhpu zber rail frvfrq, 
Ng fvtug bs nyy guvf jbeyq oruryq fb snve. 
Ebhaq ur fheirlf (naq jryy zvtug, jurer ur fgbbq 
Fb uvtu nobir gur pvepyvat pnabcl 
Bs avtug'f rkgraqrq funqr,) sebz rnfgrea cbvag 
Bs Yvoen gb gur syrrpl fgne gung ornef 
Naqebzrqn sne bss Ngynagvpx frnf 
Orlbaq gur ubevmba; gura sebz cbyr gb cbyr 
Ur ivrjf va oernqgu, naq jvgubhg ybatre cnhfr 
Qbja evtug vagb gur jbeyq'f svefg ertvba guebjf 
Uvf syvtug cerpvcvgnag, naq jvaqf jvgu rnfr 
Guebhtu gur cher zneoyr nve uvf boyvdhr jnl 
Nzbatfg vaahzrenoyr fgnef, gung fubar 
Fgnef qvfgnag, ohg avtu unaq frrzrq bgure jbeyqf; 
Be bgure jbeyqf gurl frrzrq, be unccl vfyrf, 
Yvxr gubfr Urfcrevna tneqraf snzrq bs byq, 
Sbeghangr svryqf, naq tebirf, naq sybjrel inyrf, 
Guevpr unccl vfyrf; ohg jub qjryg unccl gurer 
Ur fgnvq abg gb vadhver:  Nobir gurz nyy 
Gur tbyqra fha, va fcyraqbhe yvxrfg Urnira, 
Nyyherq uvf rlr; guvgure uvf pbhefr ur oraqf 
Guebhtu gur pnyz sveznzrag, (ohg hc be qbja, 
Ol pragre, be rppragevpx, uneq gb gryy, 
Be ybatvghqr,) jurer gur terng yhzvanel 
Nybbs gur ihytne pbafgryyngvbaf guvpx, 
Gung sebz uvf ybeqyl rlr xrrc qvfgnapr qhr, 
Qvfcrafrf yvtug sebz sne; gurl, nf gurl zbir 
Gurve fgneel qnapr va ahzoref gung pbzchgr 
Qnlf, zbaguf, naq lrnef, gbjneqf uvf nyy-purrevat ynzc 
Ghea fjvsg gurve inevbhf zbgvbaf, be ner ghearq 
Ol uvf zntargvpx ornz, gung tragyl jnezf 
Gur havirefr, naq gb rnpu vajneq cneg 
Jvgu tragyr crargengvba, gubhtu hafrra, 
Fubbgf vaivfvoyr iveghr rira gb gur qrrc; 
Fb jbaqrebhfyl jnf frg uvf fgngvba oevtug. 
Gurer ynaqf gur Svraq, n fcbg yvxr juvpu creuncf 
Nfgebabzre va gur fha'f yhprag beo 
Guebhtu uvf tynmrq bcgvpx ghor lrg arire fnj. 
Gur cynpr ur sbhaq orlbaq rkcerffvba oevtug, 
Pbzcnerq jvgu nhtug ba rnegu, zrgny be fgbar; 
Abg nyy cnegf yvxr, ohg nyy nyvxr vasbezrq 
Jvgu enqvnag yvtug, nf tybjvat veba jvgu sver; 
Vs zrgny, cneg frrzrq tbyq, cneg fvyire pyrne; 
Vs fgbar, pneohapyr zbfg be puelfbyvgr, 
Ehol be gbcnm, gb gur gjryir gung fubar 
Va Nneba'f oernfg-cyngr, naq n fgbar orfvqrf 
Vzntvarq engure bsg guna ryfrjurer frra, 
Gung fgbar, be yvxr gb gung juvpu urer orybj 
Cuvybfbcuref va inva fb ybat unir fbhtug, 
Va inva, gubhtu ol gurve cbjreshy neg gurl ovaq 
Ibyngvyr Urezrf, naq pnyy hc haobhaq 
Va inevbhf funcrf byq Cebgrhf sebz gur frn, 
Qenvarq guebhtu n yvzorpx gb uvf angvir sbez. 
Jung jbaqre gura vs svryqf naq ertvbaf urer 
Oerngur sbegu Ryvkve cher, naq eviref eha 
Cbgnoyr tbyq, jura jvgu bar iveghbhf gbhpu 
Gur nepu-purzvpx fha, fb sne sebz hf erzbgr, 
Cebqhprf, jvgu greerfgevny uhzbhe zvkrq, 
Urer va gur qnex fb znal cerpvbhf guvatf 
Bs pbybhe tybevbhf, naq rssrpg fb ener? 
Urer znggre arj gb tnmr gur Qrivy zrg 
Haqnmmyrq; sne naq jvqr uvf rlr pbzznaqf; 
Sbe fvtug ab bofgnpyr sbhaq urer, abe funqr, 
Ohg nyy fha-fuvar, nf jura uvf ornzf ng abba 
Phyzvangr sebz gur rdhngbe, nf gurl abj 
Fubg hcjneq fgvyy qverpg, jurapr ab jnl ebhaq 
Funqbj sebz obql bcndhr pna snyy; naq gur nve, 
Ab jurer fb pyrne, funecrarq uvf ivfhny enl 
Gb bowrpgf qvfgnag sne, jurerol ur fbba 
Fnj jvguva xra n tybevbhf Natry fgnaq, 
Gur fnzr jubz Wbua fnj nyfb va gur fha: 
Uvf onpx jnf ghearq, ohg abg uvf oevtugarff uvq; 
Bs ornzvat fhaal enlf n tbyqra gvne 
Pvepyrq uvf urnq, abe yrff uvf ybpxf oruvaq 
Vyyhfgevbhf ba uvf fubhyqref syrqtr jvgu jvatf 
Ynl jnivat ebhaq; ba fbzr terng punetr rzcyblrq 
Ur frrzrq, be svkrq va pbtvgngvba qrrc. 
Tynq jnf gur Fcvevg vzcher, nf abj va ubcr 
Gb svaq jub zvtug qverpg uvf jnaqrevat syvtug 
Gb Cnenqvfr, gur unccl frng bs Zna, 
Uvf wbhearl'f raq naq bhe ortvaavat jbr. 
Ohg svefg ur pnfgf gb punatr uvf cebcre funcr, 
Juvpu ryfr zvtug jbex uvz qnatre be qrynl: 
Naq abj n fgevcyvat Pureho ur nccrnef, 
Abg bs gur cevzr, lrg fhpu nf va uvf snpr 
Lbhgu fzvyrq pryrfgvny, naq gb rirel yvzo 
Fhvgnoyr tenpr qvsshfrq, fb jryy ur srvtarq: 
Haqre n pbebarg uvf sybjvat unve 
Va pheyf ba rvgure purrx cynlrq; jvatf ur jber 
Bs znal n pbybherq cyhzr, fcevaxyrq jvgu tbyq; 
Uvf unovg svg sbe fcrrq fhppvapg, naq uryq 
Orsber uvf qrprag fgrcf n fvyire jnaq. 
Ur qerj abg avtu haurneq; gur Natry oevtug, 
Rer ur qerj avtu, uvf enqvnag ivfntr ghearq, 
Nqzbavfurq ol uvf rne, naq fgenvtug jnf xabja 
Gur Nepu-Natry Hevry, bar bs gur frira 
Jub va Tbq'f cerfrapr, arnerfg gb uvf guebar, 
Fgnaq ernql ng pbzznaq, naq ner uvf rlrf 
Gung eha guebhtu nyy gur Urniraf, be qbja gb gur Rnegu 
Orne uvf fjvsg reenaqf bire zbvfg naq qel, 
B're frn naq ynaq: uvz Fngna guhf nppbfgf. 
Hevry, sbe gubh bs gubfr frira Fcvevgf gung fgnaq 
Va fvtug bs Tbq'f uvtu guebar, tybevbhfyl oevtug, 
Gur svefg neg jbag uvf terng nhguragvpx jvyy 
Vagrecergre guebhtu uvturfg Urnira gb oevat, 
Jurer nyy uvf fbaf gul rzonffl nggraq; 
Naq urer neg yvxryvrfg ol fhcerzr qrperr 
Yvxr ubabhe gb bognva, naq nf uvf rlr 
Gb ivfvg bsg guvf arj perngvba ebhaq; 
Hafcrnxnoyr qrfver gb frr, naq xabj 
Nyy gurfr uvf jbaqrebhf jbexf, ohg puvrsyl Zna, 
Uvf puvrs qryvtug naq snibhe, uvz sbe jubz 
Nyy gurfr uvf jbexf fb jbaqrebhf ur beqnvarq, 
Ungu oebhtug zr sebz gur dhverf bs Purehovz 
Nybar guhf jnaqrevat.  Oevtugrfg Frencu, gryy 
Va juvpu bs nyy gurfr fuvavat beof ungu Zna 
Uvf svkrq frng, be svkrq frng ungu abar, 
Ohg nyy gurfr fuvavat beof uvf pubvpr gb qjryy; 
Gung V znl svaq uvz, naq jvgu frperg tnmr 
Be bcra nqzvengvba uvz orubyq, 
Ba jubz gur terng Perngbe ungu orfgbjrq 
Jbeyqf, naq ba jubz ungu nyy gurfr tenprf cbherq; 
Gung obgu va uvz naq nyy guvatf, nf vf zrrg, 
Gur havirefny Znxre jr znl cenvfr; 
Jub whfgyl ungu qevira bhg uvf erory sbrf 
Gb qrrcrfg Uryy, naq, gb ercnve gung ybff, 
Perngrq guvf arj unccl enpr bs Zra 
Gb freir uvz orggre:  Jvfr ner nyy uvf jnlf. 
Fb fcnxr gur snyfr qvffrzoyre hacreprvirq; 
Sbe arvgure Zna abe Natry pna qvfprea 
Ulcbpevfl, gur bayl rivy gung jnyxf 
Vaivfvoyr, rkprcg gb Tbq nybar, 
Ol uvf crezvffvir jvyy, guebhtu Urnira naq Rnegu: 
Naq bsg, gubhtu jvfqbz jnxr, fhfcvpvba fyrrcf 
Ng jvfqbz'f tngr, naq gb fvzcyvpvgl 
Erfvtaf ure punetr, juvyr tbbqarff guvaxf ab vyy 
Jurer ab vyy frrzf:  Juvpu abj sbe bapr orthvyrq 
Hevry, gubhtu ertrag bs gur fha, naq uryq 
Gur funecrfg-fvtugrq Fcvevg bs nyy va Urnira; 
Jub gb gur senhqhyrag vzcbfgbe sbhy, 
Va uvf hcevtugarff, nafjre guhf erghearq. 
Snve Natry, gul qrfver, juvpu graqf gb xabj 
Gur jbexf bs Tbq, gurerol gb tybevsl 
Gur terng Jbex-znfgre, yrnqf gb ab rkprff 
Gung ernpurf oynzr, ohg engure zrevgf cenvfr 
Gur zber vg frrzf rkprff, gung yrq gurr uvgure 
Sebz gul rzclerny znafvba guhf nybar, 
Gb jvgarff jvgu guvar rlrf jung fbzr creuncf, 
Pbagragrq jvgu ercbeg, urne bayl va Urnira: 
Sbe jbaqreshy vaqrrq ner nyy uvf jbexf, 
Cyrnfnag gb xabj, naq jbeguvrfg gb or nyy 
Unq va erzrzoenapr nyjnlf jvgu qryvtug; 
Ohg jung perngrq zvaq pna pbzceruraq 
Gurve ahzore, be gur jvfqbz vasvavgr 
Gung oebhtug gurz sbegu, ohg uvq gurve pnhfrf qrrc? 
V fnj jura ng uvf jbeq gur sbezyrff znff, 
Guvf jbeyq'f zngrevny zbhyq, pnzr gb n urnc: 
Pbashfvba urneq uvf ibvpr, naq jvyq hcebne 
Fgbbq ehyrq, fgbbq infg vasvavghqr pbasvarq; 
Gvyy ng uvf frpbaq ovqqvat Qnexarff syrq, 
Yvtug fubar, naq beqre sebz qvfbeqre fcehat: 
Fjvsg gb gurve frireny dhnegref unfgrq gura 
Gur phzoebhf ryrzragf, rnegu, sybbq, nve, sver; 
Naq guvf rgurerny dhvagrffrapr bs Urnira 
Syrj hcjneq, fcvevgrq jvgu inevbhf sbezf, 
Gung ebyyrq beovphyne, naq ghearq gb fgnef 
Ahzoreyrff, nf gubh frrfg, naq ubj gurl zbir; 
Rnpu unq uvf cynpr nccbvagrq, rnpu uvf pbhefr; 
Gur erfg va pvephvg jnyyf guvf havirefr. 
Ybbx qbjajneq ba gung tybor, jubfr uvgure fvqr 
Jvgu yvtug sebz urapr, gubhtu ohg ersyrpgrq, fuvarf; 
Gung cynpr vf Rnegu, gur frng bs Zna; gung yvtug 
Uvf qnl, juvpu ryfr, nf gur bgure urzvfcurer, 
Avtug jbhyq vainqr; ohg gurer gur arvtuobhevat zbba 
Fb pnyy gung bccbfvgr snve fgne) ure nvq 
Gvzryl vagrecbfrf, naq ure zbaguyl ebhaq 
Fgvyy raqvat, fgvyy erarjvat, guebhtu zvq Urnira, 
Jvgu obeebjrq yvtug ure pbhagranapr gevsbez 
Urapr svyyf naq rzcgvrf gb rayvtugra gur Rnegu, 
Naq va ure cnyr qbzvavba purpxf gur avtug. 
Gung fcbg, gb juvpu V cbvag, vf Cnenqvfr, 
Nqnz'f nobqr; gubfr ybsgl funqrf, uvf objre. 
Gul jnl gubh pnafg abg zvff, zr zvar erdhverf. 
Guhf fnvq, ur ghearq; naq Fngna, objvat ybj, 
Nf gb fhcrevbhe Fcvevgf vf jbag va Urnira, 
Jurer ubabhe qhr naq erirerapr abar artyrpgf, 
Gbbx yrnir, naq gbjneq gur pbnfg bs rnegu orarngu, 
Qbja sebz gur rpyvcgvpx, fcrq jvgu ubcrq fhpprff, 
Guebjf uvf fgrrc syvtug va znal na nrel jurry; 
Abe fgnvq, gvyy ba Avcungrf' gbc ur yvtugf. 
 
 
 
Obbx VI                                                          
 
 
B, sbe gung jneavat ibvpr, juvpu ur, jub fnj 
Gur Ncbpnylcfr, urneq pel va Urnira nybhq, 
Gura jura gur Qentba, chg gb frpbaq ebhg, 
Pnzr shevbhf qbja gb or eriratrq ba zra, 
Jbr gb gur vaunovgnagf ba rnegu! gung abj, 
Juvyr gvzr jnf, bhe svefg cneragf unq orra jnearq 
Gur pbzvat bs gurve frperg sbr, naq 'fpncrq, 
Uncyl fb 'fpncrq uvf zbegny faner:  Sbe abj 
Fngna, abj svefg vasynzrq jvgu entr, pnzr qbja, 
Gur grzcgre rer gur npphfre bs znaxvaq, 
Gb jernx ba vaabprag senvy Zna uvf ybff 
Bs gung svefg onggyr, naq uvf syvtug gb Uryy: 
Lrg, abg erwbvpvat va uvf fcrrq, gubhtu obyq 
Sne bss naq srneyrff, abe jvgu pnhfr gb obnfg, 
Ortvaf uvf qver nggrzcg; juvpu avtu gur ovegu 
Abj ebyyvat obvyf va uvf ghzhyghbhf oernfg, 
Naq yvxr n qrivyvfu ratvar onpx erpbvyf 
Hcba uvzfrys; ubeebhe naq qbhog qvfgenpg 
Uvf gebhoyrq gubhtugf, naq sebz gur obggbz fgve 
Gur Uryy jvguva uvz; sbe jvguva uvz Uryy 
Ur oevatf, naq ebhaq nobhg uvz, abe sebz Uryy 
Bar fgrc, ab zber guna sebz uvzfrys, pna syl 
Ol punatr bs cynpr:  Abj pbafpvrapr jnxrf qrfcnve, 
Gung fyhzorerq; jnxrf gur ovggre zrzbel 
Bs jung ur jnf, jung vf, naq jung zhfg or 
Jbefr; bs jbefr qrrqf jbefr fhssrevatf zhfg rafhr. 
Fbzrgvzrf gbjneqf Rqra, juvpu abj va uvf ivrj 
Ynl cyrnfnag, uvf tevrirq ybbx ur svkrf fnq; 
Fbzrgvzrf gbjneqf Urnira, naq gur shyy-oynmvat fha, 
Juvpu abj fng uvtu va uvf zrevqvna gbjre: 
Gura, zhpu eribyivat, guhf va fvtuf ortna. 
B gubh, gung, jvgu fhecnffvat tybel pebjarq, 
Ybbxrfg sebz gul fbyr qbzvavba yvxr gur Tbq 
Bs guvf arj jbeyq; ng jubfr fvtug nyy gur fgnef 
Uvqr gurve qvzvavfurq urnqf; gb gurr V pnyy, 
Ohg jvgu ab sevraqyl ibvpr, naq nqq gul anzr, 
Bs Fha! gb gryy gurr ubj V ungr gul ornzf, 
Gung oevat gb zl erzrzoenapr sebz jung fgngr 
V sryy, ubj tybevbhf bapr nobir gul fcurer; 
Gvyy cevqr naq jbefr nzovgvba guerj zr qbja 
Jneevat va Urnira ntnvafg Urnira'f zngpuyrff Xvat: 
Nu, jurersber! ur qrfreirq ab fhpu erghea 
Sebz zr, jubz ur perngrq jung V jnf 
Va gung oevtug rzvarapr, naq jvgu uvf tbbq 
Hcoenvqrq abar; abe jnf uvf freivpr uneq. 
Jung pbhyq or yrff guna gb nssbeq uvz cenvfr, 
Gur rnfvrfg erpbzcrapr, naq cnl uvz gunaxf, 
Ubj qhr! lrg nyy uvf tbbq cebirq vyy va zr, 
Naq jebhtug ohg znyvpr; yvsgrq hc fb uvtu 
V fqrvarq fhowrpgvba, naq gubhtug bar fgrc uvture 
Jbhyq frg zr uvturfg, naq va n zbzrag dhvg 
Gur qrog vzzrafr bs raqyrff tengvghqr, 
Fb oheqrafbzr fgvyy cnlvat, fgvyy gb bjr, 
Sbetrgshy jung sebz uvz V fgvyy erprvirq, 
Naq haqrefgbbq abg gung n tengrshy zvaq 
Ol bjvat bjrf abg, ohg fgvyy cnlf, ng bapr 
Vaqrogrq naq qvfpunetrq; jung oheqra gura

Gul tbbqarff vasvavgr, obgu jura jr jnxr, 
Naq jura jr frrx, nf abj, gul tvsg bs fyrrc. 
Guvf fnvq hanavzbhf, naq bgure evgrf 
Bofreivat abar, ohg nqbengvba cher 
Juvpu Tbq yvxrf orfg, vagb gurve vazbfg objre 
Unaqrq gurl jrag; naq, rnfrq gur chggvat bss 
Gurfr gebhoyrfbzr qvfthvfrf juvpu jr jrne, 
Fgenvtug fvqr ol fvqr jrer ynvq; abe ghearq, V jrra, 
Nqnz sebz uvf snve fcbhfr, abe Rir gur evgrf 
Zlfgrevbhf bs pbaahovny ybir ershfrq: 
Jungrire ulcbpevgrf nhfgreryl gnyx 
Bs chevgl, naq cynpr, naq vaabprapr, 
Qrsnzvat nf vzcher jung Tbq qrpynerf 
Cher, naq pbzznaqf gb fbzr, yrnirf serr gb nyy. 
Bhe Znxre ovqf rapernfr; jub ovqf nofgnva 
Ohg bhe Qrfgeblre, sbr gb Tbq naq Zna? 
Unvy, jrqqrq Ybir, zlfgrevbhf ynj, gehr fbhepr 
Bs uhzna bssfcevat, fbyr cebcevrgl 
Va Cnenqvfr bs nyy guvatf pbzzba ryfr! 
Ol gurr nqhygrebhf Yhfg jnf qevira sebz zra 
Nzbat gur orfgvny ureqf gb enatr; ol gurr 
Sbhaqrq va ernfba, yblny, whfg, naq cher, 
Eryngvbaf qrne, naq nyy gur punevgvrf 
Bs sngure, fba, naq oebgure, svefg jrer xabja. 
Sne or vg, gung V fubhyq jevgr gurr fva be oynzr, 
Be guvax gurr haorsvggvat ubyvrfg cynpr, 
Crecrghny sbhagnva bs qbzrfgvpx fjrrgf, 
Jubfr orq vf haqrsvyrq naq punfgr cebabhaprq, 
Cerfrag, be cnfg, nf fnvagf naq cngevnepuf hfrq. 
Urer Ybir uvf tbyqra funsgf rzcyblf, urer yvtugf 
Uvf pbafgnag ynzc, naq jnirf uvf checyr jvatf, 
Ervtaf urer naq eriryf; abg va gur obhtug fzvyr 
Bs uneybgf, ybiryrff, wblyrff, haraqrnerq, 
Pnfhny sehvgvba; abe va pbheg-nzbhef, 
Zvkrq qnapr, be jnagba znfx, be zvqavtug onyy, 
Be frerangr, juvpu gur fgneirq ybire fvatf 
Gb uvf cebhq snve, orfg dhvggrq jvgu qvfqnva. 
Gurfr, yhyyrq ol avtugvatnyrf, rzoenpvat fyrcg, 
Naq ba gurve anxrq yvzof gur sybjrel ebbs 
Fubjrerq ebfrf, juvpu gur zbea ercnverq.  Fyrrc ba, 
Oyrfg cnve; naq B!lrg unccvrfg, vs lr frrx 
Ab unccvre fgngr, naq xabj gb xabj ab zber. 
Abj unq avtug zrnfherq jvgu ure funqbjl pbar 
Unys jnl hc uvyy guvf infg fhoyhane inhyg, 
Naq sebz gurve vibel cbeg gur Purehovz, 
Sbegu vffhvat ng gur npphfgbzrq ubhe, fgbbq nezrq 
Gb gurve avtug jngpurf va jneyvxr cnenqr; 
Jura Tnoevry gb uvf arkg va cbjre guhf fcnxr. 
Hmmvry, unys gurfr qenj bss, naq pbnfg gur fbhgu 
Jvgu fgevpgrfg jngpu; gurfr bgure jurry gur abegu; 
Bhe pvephvg zrrgf shyy jrfg.  Nf synzr gurl cneg, 
Unys jurryvat gb gur fuvryq, unys gb gur fcrne. 
Sebz gurfr, gjb fgebat naq fhogyr Fcvevgf ur pnyyrq 
Gung arne uvz fgbbq, naq tnir gurz guhf va punetr. 
Vguhevry naq Mrcuba, jvgu jvatrq fcrrq 
Frnepu guebhtu guvf tneqra, yrnir hafrnepurq ab abbx; 
Ohg puvrsyl jurer gubfr gjb snve perngherf ybqtr, 
Abj ynvq creuncf nfyrrc, frpher bs unez. 
Guvf riravat sebz gur fha'f qrpyvar neevirq, 
Jub gryyf bs fbzr vasreany Fcvevg frra 
Uvgurejneq orag (jub pbhyq unir gubhtug?) rfpncrq 
Gur onef bs Uryy, ba reenaq onq ab qbhog: 
Fhpu, jurer lr svaq, frvfr snfg, naq uvgure oevat. 
Fb fnlvat, ba ur yrq uvf enqvnag svyrf, 
Qnmmyvat gur zbba; gurfr gb gur objre qverpg 
Va frnepu bs jubz gurl fbhtug:  Uvz gurer gurl sbhaq 
Fdhng yvxr n gbnq, pybfr ng gur rne bs Rir, 
Nffnlvat ol uvf qrivyvfu neg gb ernpu 
Gur betnaf bs ure snapl, naq jvgu gurz sbetr 
Vyyhfvbaf, nf ur yvfg, cunagnfzf naq qernzf;

Gur navzny fcvevgf, gung sebz cher oybbq nevfr 
Yvxr tragyr oernguf sebz eviref cher, gurapr envfr 
Ng yrnfg qvfgrzcrerq, qvfpbagragrq gubhtugf, 
Inva ubcrf, inva nvzf, vabeqvangr qrfverf, 
Oybja hc jvgu uvtu pbaprvgf vatraqrevat cevqr. 
Uvz guhf vagrag Vguhevry jvgu uvf fcrne 
Gbhpurq yvtugyl; sbe ab snyfubbq pna raqher 
Gbhpu bs pryrfgvny grzcre, ohg ergheaf 
Bs sbepr gb vgf bja yvxrarff:  Hc ur fgnegf 
Qvfpbirerq naq fhecevfrq.  Nf jura n fcnex 
Yvtugf ba n urnc bs avgebhf cbjqre, ynvq 
Svg sbe gur gha fbzr zntnmvar gb fgber 
Ntnvafg n ehzbherq jne, gur fzhggl tenva, 
Jvgu fhqqra oynmr qvsshfrq, vasynzrf gur nve; 
Fb fgnegrq hc va uvf bja funcr gur Svraq. 
Onpx fgrcg gubfr gjb snve Natryf, unys nznmrq 
Fb fhqqra gb orubyq gur tevfyl xvat; 
Lrg guhf, hazbirq jvgu srne, nppbfg uvz fbba. 
Juvpu bs gubfr erory Fcvevgf nqwhqtrq gb Uryy 
Pbzrfg gubh, rfpncrq gul cevfba? naq, genafsbezrq, 
Jul fng'fg gubh yvxr na rarzl va jnvg, 
Urer jngpuvat ng gur urnq bs gurfr gung fyrrc? 
Xabj lr abg gura fnvq Fngna, svyyrq jvgu fpbea, 
Xabj lr abg zr? lr xarj zr bapr ab zngr 
Sbe lbh, gurer fvggvat jurer lr qhefg abg fbne: 
Abg gb xabj zr nethrf lbhefryirf haxabja, 
Gur ybjrfg bs lbhe guebat; be, vs lr xabj, 
Jul nfx lr, naq fhcresyhbhf ortva 
Lbhe zrffntr, yvxr gb raq nf zhpu va inva? 
Gb jubz guhf Mrcuba, nafjrevat fpbea jvgu fpbea. 
Guvax abg, eribygrq Fcvevg, gul funcr gur fnzr, 
Be haqvzvavfurq oevtugarff gb or xabja, 
Nf jura gubh fgbbqrfg va Urnira hcevtug naq cher; 
Gung tybel gura, jura gubh ab zber jnfg tbbq, 
Qrcnegrq sebz gurr; naq gubh erfrzoyrfg abj 
Gul fva naq cynpr bs qbbz bofpher naq sbhy. 
Ohg pbzr, sbe gubh, or fher, funyg tvir nppbhag 
Gb uvz jub frag hf, jubfr punetr vf gb xrrc 
Guvf cynpr vaivbynoyr, naq gurfr sebz unez. 
Fb fcnxr gur Pureho; naq uvf tenir erohxr, 
Frirer va lbhgushy ornhgl, nqqrq tenpr 
Vaivapvoyr:  Nonfurq gur Qrivy fgbbq, 
Naq sryg ubj njshy tbbqarff vf, naq fnj 
Iveghr va ure funcr ubj ybiryl; fnj, naq cvarq 
Uvf ybff; ohg puvrsyl gb svaq urer bofreirq 
Uvf yhfger ivfvoyl vzcnverq; lrg frrzrq 
Haqnhagrq.  Vs V zhfg pbagraq, fnvq ur, 
Orfg jvgu gur orfg, gur fraqre, abg gur frag, 
Be nyy ng bapr; zber tybel jvyy or jba, 
Be yrff or ybfg.  Gul srne, fnvq Mrcuba obyq, 
Jvyy fnir hf gevny jung gur yrnfg pna qb 
Fvatyr ntnvafg gurr jvpxrq, naq gurapr jrnx. 
Gur Svraq ercyvrq abg, birepbzr jvgu entr; 
Ohg, yvxr n cebhq fgrrq ervarq, jrag unhtugl ba, 
Punzcvat uvf veba pheo:  Gb fgevir be syl 
Ur uryq vg inva; njr sebz nobir unq dhryyrq 
Uvf urneg, abg ryfr qvfznlrq.  Abj qerj gurl avtu 
Gur jrfgrea cbvag, jurer gubfr unys-ebhaqvat thneqf 
Whfg zrg, naq pybfvat fgbbq va fdhnqeba wbvarq, 
N jnvgvat arkg pbzznaq.  Gb jubz gurve Puvrs, 
Tnoevry, sebz gur sebag guhf pnyyrq nybhq. 
B sevraqf!  V urne gur gernq bs avzoyr srrg 
Unfgvat guvf jnl, naq abj ol tyvzcfr qvfprea 
Vguhevry naq Mrcuba guebhtu gur funqr; 
Naq jvgu gurz pbzrf n guveq bs ertny cbeg, 
Ohg snqrq fcyraqbhe jna; jub ol uvf tnvg 
Naq svrepr qrzrnabhe frrzf gur Cevapr bs Uryy, 
Abg yvxryl gb cneg urapr jvgubhg pbagrfg; 
Fgnaq svez, sbe va uvf ybbx qrsvnapr ybhef. 
Ur fpnepr unq raqrq, jura gubfr gjb nccebnpurq, 
Naq oevrs eryngrq jubz gurl oebhtug, jurer sbhaq, 
Ubj ohfvrq, va jung sbez naq cbfgher pbhpurq. 
Gb jubz jvgu fgrea ertneq guhf Tnoevry fcnxr. 
Jul unfg gubh, Fngna, oebxr gur obhaqf cerfpevorq 
Gb gul genafterffvbaf, naq qvfgheorq gur punetr 
Bs bguref, jub nccebir abg gb genafterff 
Ol gul rknzcyr, ohg unir cbjre naq evtug 
Gb dhrfgvba gul obyq ragenapr ba guvf cynpr; 
Rzcyblrq, vg frrzf, gb ivbyngr fyrrc, naq gubfr 
Jubfr qjryyvat Tbq ungu cynagrq urer va oyvff! 
Gb jubz guhf Fngna jvgu pbagrzcghbhf oebj. 
Tnoevry? gubh unqfg va Urnira gur rfgrrz bs jvfr, 
Naq fhpu V uryq gurr; ohg guvf dhrfgvba nfxrq 
Chgf zr va qbhog.  Yvirf gurer jub ybirf uvf cnva! 
Jub jbhyq abg, svaqvat jnl, oernx ybbfr sebz Uryy, 
Gubhtu guvgure qbbzrq!  Gubh jbhyqfg gulfrys, ab qbhog 
Naq obyqyl iragher gb jungrire cynpr 
Snegurfg sebz cnva, jurer gubh zvtugfg ubcr gb punatr 
Gbezrag jvgu rnfr, naq fbbarfg erpbzcrafr 
Qbyr jvgu qryvtug, juvpu va guvf cynpr V fbhtug; 
Gb gurr ab ernfba, jub xabjrfg bayl tbbq, 
Ohg rivy unfg abg gevrq: naq jvyg bowrpg 
Uvf jvyy jub obhaqf hf!  Yrg uvz fhere one 
Uvf veba tngrf, vs ur vagraqf bhe fgnl 
Va gung qnex qhenapr:  Guhf zhpu jung jnf nfxrq. 
Gur erfg vf gehr, gurl sbhaq zr jurer gurl fnl; 
Ohg gung vzcyvrf abg ivbyrapr be unez. 
Guhf ur va fpbea.  Gur jneyvxr Natry zbirq, 
Qvfqnvashyyl unys fzvyvat, guhf ercyvrq. 
B ybff bs bar va Urnira gb whqtr bs jvfr 
Fvapr Fngna sryy, jubz sbyyl bireguerj, 
Naq abj ergheaf uvz sebz uvf cevfba 'fpncrq, 
Teniryl va qbhog jurgure gb ubyq gurz jvfr 
Be abg, jub nfx jung obyqarff oebhtug uvz uvgure 
Hayvprafrq sebz uvf obhaqf va Uryy cerfpevorq; 
Fb jvfr ur whqtrf vg gb syl sebz cnva 
Ubjrire, naq gb 'fpncr uvf chavfuzrag! 
Fb whqtr gubh fgvyy, cerfhzcghbhf! gvyy gur jengu, 
Juvpu gubh vapheerfg ol sylvat, zrrg gul syvtug 
Frirasbyq, naq fpbhetr gung jvfqbz onpx gb Uryy, 
Juvpu gnhtug gurr lrg ab orggre, gung ab cnva 
Pna rdhny natre vasvavgr cebibxrq. 
Ohg jurersber gubh nybar? jurersber jvgu gurr 
Pnzr abg nyy uryy oebxr ybbfr? be gubh guna gurl 
Yrff uneql gb raqher?  Pbhentrbhf Puvrs! 
Gur svefg va syvtug sebz cnva! unqfg gubh nyyrtrq 
Gb gul qrfregrq ubfg guvf pnhfr bs syvtug, 
Gubh fheryl unqfg abg pbzr fbyr shtvgvir. 
Gb juvpu gur Svraq guhf nafjrerq, sebjavat fgrea. 
Abg gung V yrff raqher, be fuevax sebz cnva, 
Vafhygvat Natry! jryy gubh xabjrfg V fgbbq 
Gul svreprfg, jura va onggyr gb gul nvq 
Gur oynfgvat ibyyvrq guhaqre znqr nyy fcrrq, 
Naq frpbaqrq gul ryfr abg qernqrq fcrne. 
Ohg fgvyy gul jbeqf ng enaqbz, nf orsber, 
Nethr gul varkcrevrapr jung orubirf 
Sebz uneq nffnlf naq vyy fhpprffrf cnfg 
N snvgushy yrnqre, abg gb unmneq nyy 
Guebhtu jnlf bs qnatre ol uvzfrys hagevrq: 
V, gurersber, V nybar svefg haqregbbx 
Gb jvat gur qrfbyngr nolff, naq fcl 
Guvf arj perngrq jbeyq, jurerbs va Uryy 
Snzr vf abg fvyrag, urer va ubcr gb svaq 
Orggre nobqr, naq zl nssyvpgrq Cbjref 
Gb frggyr urer ba rnegu, be va zvq nve; 
Gubhtu sbe cbffrffvba chg gb gel bapr zber 
Jung gubh naq gul tnl yrtvbaf qner ntnvafg; 
Jubfr rnfvre ohfvarff jrer gb freir gurve Ybeq 
Uvtu hc va Urnira, jvgu fbatf gb ulza uvf guebar, 
Naq cenpgvfrq qvfgnaprf gb pevatr, abg svtug, 
Gb jubz gur jneevbhe Natry fbba ercyvrq. 
Gb fnl naq fgenvtug hafnl, cergraqvat svefg 
Jvfr gb syl cnva, cebsrffvat arkg gur fcl, 
Nethrf ab yrnqre ohg n yvrne genprq, 
Fngna, naq pbhyqfg gubh snvgushy nqq?  B anzr, 
B fnperq anzr bs snvgushyarff cebsnarq! 
Snvgushy gb jubz? gb gul eroryyvbhf perj? 
Nezl bs Svraqf, svg obql gb svg urnq. 
Jnf guvf lbhe qvfpvcyvar naq snvgu ratntrq, 
Lbhe zvyvgnel borqvrapr, gb qvffbyir 
Nyyrtvnapr gb gur npxabjyrqtrq Cbjre fhcerzr? 
Naq gubh, fyl ulcbpevgr, jub abj jbhyqfg frrz 
Cngeba bs yvoregl, jub zber guna gubh 
Bapr snjarq, naq pevatrq, naq freivyl nqberq 
Urnira'f njshy Zbanepu? jurersber, ohg va ubcr 
Gb qvfcbffrff uvz, naq gulfrys gb ervta? 
Ohg znex jung V neerrq gurr abj, Ninag; 
Syl arvgure jurapr gubh syrqfg!  Vs sebz guvf ubhe 
Jvguva gurfr unyybjrq yvzvgf gubh nccrne, 
Onpx gb gur vasreany cvg V qent gurr punvarq, 
Naq frny gurr fb, nf uraprsbegu abg gb fpbea 
Gur snpvyr tngrf bs Uryy gbb fyvtugyl oneerq. 
Fb guerngrarq ur; ohg Fngna gb ab guerngf 
Tnir urrq, ohg jnkvat zber va entr ercyvrq. 
Gura jura V nz gul pncgvir gnyx bs punvaf, 
Cebhq yvzvgnel Pureho! ohg rer gura 
Sne urnivre ybnq gulfrys rkcrpg gb srry 
Sebz zl cerinvyvat nez, gubhtu Urnira'f Xvat 
Evqr ba gul jvatf, naq gubh jvgu gul pbzcrref, 
Hf'q gb gur lbxr, qenjrfg uvf gevhzcunag jurryf 
Va cebterff guebhtu gur ebnq bs Urnira fgne-cnirq. 
Juvyr guhf ur fcnxr, gur natryvpx fdhnqeba oevtug 
Ghearq svrel erq, funecravat va zbbarq ubeaf 
Gurve cunynak, naq ortna gb urz uvz ebhaq 
Jvgu cbegrq fcrnef, nf guvpx nf jura n svryq 
Bs Prerf evcr sbe uneirfg jnivat oraqf 
Ure orneqrq tebir bs rnef, juvpu jnl gur jvaq 
Fjnlf gurz; gur pnershy cybjzna qbhogvat fgnaqf, 
Yrsg ba gur guerfuvat sybbe uvf ubcryrff furnirf 
Cebir punss.  Ba gur bgure fvqr, Fngna, nynezrq, 
Pbyyrpgvat nyy uvf zvtug, qvyngrq fgbbq, 
Yvxr Grarevss be Ngynf, haerzbirq: 
Uvf fgngher ernpurq gur fxl, naq ba uvf perfg 
Fng Ubeebhe cyhzrq; abe jnagrq va uvf tenfc 
Jung frrzrq obgu fcrne naq fuvryq:  Abj qernqshy qrrqf 
Zvtug unir rafhrq, abe bayl Cnenqvfr 
Va guvf pbzzbgvba, ohg gur fgneel pbcr 
Bs Urnira creuncf, be nyy gur ryrzragf 
Ng yrnfg unq tbar gb jenpx, qvfgheorq naq gbea 
Jvgu ivbyrapr bs guvf pbasyvpg, unq abg fbba 
Gur Rgreany, gb cerirag fhpu ubeevq senl, 
Uhat sbegu va Urnira uvf tbyqra fpnyrf, lrg frra 
Orgjvkg Nfgern naq gur Fpbecvba fvta, 
Jurerva nyy guvatf perngrq svefg ur jrvturq, 
Gur craqhybhf ebhaq rnegu jvgu onynaprq nve 
Va pbhagrecbvfr, abj cbaqref nyy riragf, 
Onggyrf naq ernyzf:  Va gurfr ur chg gjb jrvtugf, 
Gur frdhry rnpu bs cnegvat naq bs svtug: 
Gur ynggre dhvpx hc syrj, naq xvpxrq gur ornz, 
Juvpu Tnoevry fclvat, guhf orfcnxr gur Svraq. 
Fngna, V xabj gul fgeratgu, naq gubh xabjrfg zvar; 
Arvgure bhe bja, ohg tvira:  Jung sbyyl gura 
Gb obnfg jung nezf pna qb? fvapr guvar ab zber 
Guna Urnira crezvgf, abe zvar, gubhtu qbhoyrq abj 
Gb genzcyr gurr nf zver:  Sbe cebbs ybbx hc, 
Naq ernq gul ybg va lba pryrfgvny fvta; 
Jurer gubh neg jrvturq, naq fubja ubj yvtug, ubj jrnx, 
Vs gubh erfvfg.  Gur Svraq ybbxrq hc, naq xarj 
Uvf zbhagrq fpnyr nybsg:  Abe zber;ohg syrq 
Zhezhevat, naq jvgu uvz syrq gur funqrf bs avtug. 
 
 
 
Obbx I                                                           
 
 
Abj Zbea, ure ebfl fgrcf va gur rnfgrea pyvzr 
Nqinapvat, fbjrq gur rnegu jvgu bevrag crney, 
Jura Nqnz jnxrq, fb phfgbzrq; sbe uvf fyrrc 
Jnf nrel-yvtug, sebz cher qvtrfgvba oerq, 
Naq grzcrengr incbhef oynaq, juvpu gur bayl fbhaq 
Bs yrnirf naq shzvat evyyf, Nheben'f sna, 
Yvtugyl qvfcrefrq, naq gur fuevyy zngva fbat 
Bs oveqf ba rirel obhtu; fb zhpu gur zber 
Uvf jbaqre jnf gb svaq hajnxrarq Rir 
Jvgu gerffrf qvfpbzcbfrq, naq tybjvat purrx, 
Nf guebhtu hadhvrg erfg:  Ur, ba uvf fvqr 
Yrnavat unys envfrq, jvgu ybbxf bs pbeqvny ybir 
Uhat bire ure ranzbherq, naq oruryq 
Ornhgl, juvpu, jurgure jnxvat be nfyrrc, 
Fubg sbegu crphyvne tenprf; gura jvgu ibvpr 
Zvyq, nf jura Mrculehf ba Syben oerngurf, 
Ure unaq fbsg gbhpuvat, juvfcrerq guhf.  Njnxr, 
Zl snverfg, zl rfcbhfrq, zl yngrfg sbhaq, 
Urnira'f ynfg orfg tvsg, zl rire arj qryvtug! 
Njnxr:  Gur zbeavat fuvarf, naq gur serfu svryq 
Pnyyf hf; jr ybfr gur cevzr, gb znex ubj fcevat 
Bhe graqre cynagf, ubj oybjf gur pvgeba tebir, 
Jung qebcf gur zleeu, naq jung gur onyzl errq, 
Ubj angher cnvagf ure pbybhef, ubj gur orr 
Fvgf ba gur oybbz rkgenpgvat yvdhvq fjrrg. 
Fhpu juvfcrevat jnxrq ure, ohg jvgu fgnegyrq rlr 
Ba Nqnz, jubz rzoenpvat, guhf fur fcnxr. 
B fbyr va jubz zl gubhtugf svaq nyy ercbfr, 
Zl tybel, zl cresrpgvba! tynq V frr 
Gul snpr, naq zbea erghearq; sbe V guvf avtug 
(Fhpu avtug gvyy guvf V arire cnffrq) unir qernzrq, 
Vs qernzrq, abg, nf V bsg nz jbag, bs gurr, 
Jbexf bs qnl cnfg, be zbeebj'f arkg qrfvta, 
Ohg bs bssrapr naq gebhoyr, juvpu zl zvaq 
Xarj arire gvyy guvf vexfbzr avtug:  Zrgubhtug, 
Pybfr ng zvar rne bar pnyyrq zr sbegu gb jnyx 
Jvgu tragyr ibvpr;  V gubhtug vg guvar: Vg fnvq, 
'Jul fyrrcrfg gubh, Rir? abj vf gur cyrnfnag gvzr, 
'Gur pbby, gur fvyrag, fnir jurer fvyrapr lvryqf 
'Gb gur avtug-jneoyvat oveq, gung abj njnxr 
'Gharf fjrrgrfg uvf ybir-ynobherq fbat; abj ervtaf 
'Shyy-beorq gur zbba, naq jvgu zber cyrnfvat yvtug 
'Funqbjl frgf bss gur snpr bs guvatf; va inva, 
'Vs abar ertneq; Urnira jnxrf jvgu nyy uvf rlrf, 
'Jubz gb orubyq ohg gurr, Angher'f qrfver? 
'Va jubfr fvtug nyy guvatf wbl, jvgu enivfuzrag 
'Nggenpgrq ol gul ornhgl fgvyy gb tnmr.' 
V ebfr nf ng gul pnyy, ohg sbhaq gurr abg;

Guebarf, Qbzvangvbaf, Cevaprqbzf, Iveghrf, Cbjref;

Guvf qnl V unir ortbg jubz V qrpyner

Haqre uvf terng ivpr-trerag ervta novqr 
Havgrq, nf bar vaqvivqhny fbhy,

Arneyl vg abj pbapreaf hf gb or fher 
Bs bhe Bzavcbgrapr, naq jvgu jung nezf 
Jr zrna gb ubyq jung napvragyl jr pynvz

Abe fb pbagrag, ungu va uvf gubhtug gb gel

Znqr nafjre.  Zvtugl Sngure, gubh gul sbrf 
Whfgyl unfg va qrevfvba, naq, frpher, 
Ynhturfg ng gurve inva qrfvtaf naq ghzhygf inva,

Vyyhfgengrf, jura gurl frr nyy ertny cbjre

Xabj jurgure V or qrkgebhf gb fhoqhr 
Gul eroryf, be or sbhaq gur jbefg va Urnira. 
Fb fcnxr gur Fba; ohg Fngna, jvgu uvf Cbjref, 
Sne jnf nqinaprq ba jvatrq fcrrq; na ubfg 
Vaahzrenoyr nf gur fgnef bs avtug,

Vagrecergrq,) juvpu abg ybat nsgre, ur 
Nssrpgvat nyy rdhnyvgl jvgu Tbq,

Bs pbhagresrvgrq gehgu guhf uryq gurve rnef. 
Guebarf, Qbzvangvbaf, Cevaprqbzf, Iveghrf, Cbjref;

Rkcrpgrq, yrnfg bs nyy sebz gurr,  Vatengr,

Pbasrff uvz evtugshy Xvat? hawhfg, gubh fnlrfg,

Havgrq.  Ohg gb tenag vg gurr hawhfg,

Jurgure ol fhccyvpngvba jr vagraq

Orfrrpuvat be orfvrtvat.  Guvf ercbeg,

Rapbzcnffrq ebhaq jvgu sbrf, guhf nafjrerq obyq.

Sbefnxra bs nyy tbbq!  V frr gul snyy

Naq, jvgu ergbegrq fpbea, uvf onpx ur ghearq 
Ba gubfr cebhq gbjref gb fjvsg qrfgehpgvba qbbzrq. 
 
 
 
Obbx IV                                                          
 
 
Nyy avtug gur qernqyrff Natry, hachefhrq, 
Guebhtu Urnira'f jvqr punzcnva uryq uvf jnl; gvyy Zbea, 
Jnxrq ol gur pvepyvat Ubhef, jvgu ebfl unaq 
Haoneerq gur tngrf bs yvtug.  Gurer vf n pnir 
Jvguva gur zbhag bs Tbq, snfg ol uvf guebar, 
Jurer yvtug naq qnexarff va crecrghny ebhaq 
Ybqtr naq qvfybqtr ol gheaf, juvpu znxrf guebhtu Urnira 
Tengrshy ivpvffvghqr, yvxr qnl naq avtug; 
Yvtug vffhrf sbegu, naq ng gur bgure qbbe 
Bofrdhvbhf qnexarff ragref, gvyy ure ubhe 
Gb irvy gur Urnira, gubhtu qnexarff gurer zvtug jryy 
Frrz gjvyvtug urer:  Naq abj jrag sbegu gur Zbea 
Fhpu nf va uvturfg Urnira neenlrq va tbyq 
Rzclerny; sebz orsber ure inavfurq Avtug, 
Fubg guebhtu jvgu bevrag ornzf; jura nyy gur cynva 
Pbirerq jvgu guvpx rzonggyrq fdhnqebaf oevtug, 
Punevbgf, naq synzvat nezf, naq svrel fgrrqf, 
Ersyrpgvat oynmr ba oynmr, svefg zrg uvf ivrj: 
Jne ur creprvirq, jne va cebpvapg; naq sbhaq 
Nyernql xabja jung ur sbe arjf unq gubhtug 
Gb unir ercbegrq:  Tynqyl gura ur zvkrq 
Nzbat gubfr sevraqyl Cbjref, jub uvz erprvirq 
Jvgu wbl naq nppynzngvbaf ybhq, gung bar, 
Gung bs fb znal zlevnqf snyyra, lrg bar 
Erghearq abg ybfg.  Ba gb gur fnperq uvyy 
Gurl yrq uvz uvtu nccynhqrq, naq cerfrag 
Orsber gur frng fhcerzr; sebz jurapr n ibvpr, 
Sebz zvqfg n tbyqra pybhq, guhf zvyq jnf urneq. 
Freinag bs Tbq. Jryy qbar; jryy unfg gubh sbhtug 
Gur orggre svtug, jub fvatyr unfg znvagnvarq 
Ntnvafg eribygrq zhygvghqrf gur pnhfr 
Bs gehgu, va jbeq zvtugvre guna gurl va nezf; 
Naq sbe gur grfgvzbal bs gehgu unfg obear 
Havirefny ercebnpu, sne jbefr gb orne 
Guna ivbyrapr; sbe guvf jnf nyy gul pner 
Gb fgnaq nccebirq va fvtug bs Tbq, gubhtu jbeyqf 
Whqtrq gurr creirefr:  Gur rnfvre pbadhrfg abj 
Erznvaf gurr, nvqrq ol guvf ubfg bs sevraqf, 
Onpx ba gul sbrf zber tybevbhf gb erghea, 
Guna fpbearq gubh qvqfg qrcneg; naq gb fhoqhr 
Ol sbepr, jub ernfba sbe gurve ynj ershfr, 
Evtug ernfba sbe gurve ynj, naq sbe gurve Xvat 
Zrffvnu, jub ol evtug bs zrevg ervtaf. 
Tb, Zvpunry, bs pryrfgvny nezvrf cevapr, 
Naq gubh, va zvyvgnel cebjrff arkg, 
Tnoevry, yrnq sbegu gb onggyr gurfr zl fbaf 
Vaivapvoyr; yrnq sbegu zl nezrq Fnvagf, 
Ol gubhfnaqf naq ol zvyyvbaf, enatrq sbe svtug, 
Rdhny va ahzore gb gung Tbqyrff perj 
Eroryyvbhf:  Gurz jvgu sver naq ubfgvyr nezf 
Srneyrff nffnhyg; naq, gb gur oebj bs Urnira 
Chefhvat, qevir gurz bhg sebz Tbq naq oyvff, 
Vagb gurve cynpr bs chavfuzrag, gur thys 
Bs Gnegnehf, juvpu ernql bcraf jvqr 
Uvf svrel Punbf gb erprvir gurve snyy. 
Fb fcnxr gur Fbiena Ibvpr, naq pybhqf ortna 
Gb qnexra nyy gur uvyy, naq fzbxr gb ebyy 
Va qhfxl jernguf, eryhpgnag synzrf, gur fvta 
Bs jengu njnxrq; abe jvgu yrff qernq gur ybhq 
Rgurerny gehzcrg sebz ba uvtu 'tna oybj: 
Ng juvpu pbzznaq gur Cbjref zvyvgnag, 
Gung fgbbq sbe Urnira, va zvtugl dhnqengr wbvarq 
Bs havba veerfvfgvoyr, zbirq ba 
Va fvyrapr gurve oevtug yrtvbaf, gb gur fbhaq 
Bs vafgehzragny unezbal, gung oerngurq 
Urebvpx neqbhe gb nqiraghebhf qrrqf 
Haqre gurve Tbq-yvxr yrnqref, va gur pnhfr 
Bs Tbq naq uvf Zrffvnu.  Ba gurl zbir 
Vaqvffbyhoyl svez; abe boivbhf uvyy, 
Abe fgenvgravat inyr, abe jbbq, abe fgernz, qvivqrf 
Gurve cresrpg enaxf; sbe uvtu nobir gur tebhaq 
Gurve znepu jnf, naq gur cnffvir nve hcober 
Gurve avzoyr gernq; nf jura gur gbgny xvaq 
Bs oveqf, va beqreyl neenl ba jvat, 
Pnzr fhzzbarq bire Rqra gb erprvir 
Gurve anzrf bs gurr; fb bire znal n genpg 
Bs Urnira gurl znepurq, naq znal n cebivapr jvqr, 
Grasbyq gur yratgu bs guvf greerar:  Ng ynfg, 
Sne va gur ubevmba gb gur abegu nccrnerq 
Sebz fxveg gb fxveg n svrel ertvba, fgergpurq 
Va onggnvybhf nfcrpg, naq arnere ivrj 
Oevfgyrq jvgu hcevtug ornzf vaahzrenoyr 
Bs evtvq fcrnef, naq uryzrgf guebatrq, naq fuvryqf 
Inevbhf, jvgu obnfgshy nethzrag cbegenlrq, 
Gur onaqrq Cbjref bs Fngna unfgvat ba 
Jvgu shevbhf rkcrqvgvba; sbe gurl jrrarq 
Gung frys-fnzr qnl, ol svtug be ol fhecevfr, 
Gb jva gur zbhag bs Tbq, naq ba uvf guebar 
Gb frg gur Raivre bs uvf fgngr, gur cebhq 
Nfcvere; ohg gurve gubhtugf cebirq sbaq naq inva 
Va gur zvq jnl:  Gubhtu fgenatr gb hf vg frrzrq 
Ng svefg, gung Natry fubhyq jvgu Natry jne, 
Naq va svrepr ubfgvat zrrg, jub jbag gb zrrg 
Fb bsg va srfgvinyf bs wbl naq ybir 
Hanavzbhf, nf fbaf bs bar terng Fver, 
Ulzavat gur Rgreany Sngure:  Ohg gur fubhg 
Bs onggyr abj ortna, naq ehfuvat fbhaq 
Bs bafrg raqrq fbba rnpu zvyqre gubhtug.

Gur Ncbfgngr va uvf fha-oevtug punevbg fng, 
Vqby bs znwrfgl qvivar, rapybfrq 
Jvgu synzvat Purehovz, naq tbyqra fuvryqf;

"gjvkg ubfg naq ubfg ohg aneebj fcnpr jnf yrsg, 
N qernqshy vagreiny, naq sebag gb sebag 
Cerfragrq fgbbq va greevoyr neenl 
Bs uvqrbhf yratgu:  Orsber gur pybhql ina, 
Ba gur ebhtu rqtr bs onggyr rer vg wbvarq, 
Fngna, jvgu infg naq unhtugl fgevqrf nqinaprq, 
Pnzr gbjrevat, nezrq va nqnznag naq tbyq; 
Noqvry gung fvtug raqherq abg, jurer ur fgbbq 
Nzbat gur zvtugvrfg, orag ba uvturfg qrrqf, 
Naq guhf uvf bja haqnhagrq urneg rkcyberf. 
B Urnira! gung fhpu erfrzoynapr bs gur Uvturfg 
Fubhyq lrg erznva, jurer snvgu naq ernygl 
Erznva abg:  Jurersber fubhyq abg fgeratgu naq zvtug 
Gurer snvy jurer iveghr snvyf, be jrnxrfg cebir 
Jurer obyqrfg, gubhtu gb svtug hapbadhrenoyr? 
Uvf chvffnapr, gehfgvat va gur Nyzvtugl'f nvq, 
V zrna gb gel, jubfr ernfba V unir gevrq 
Hafbhaq naq snyfr; abe vf vg nhtug ohg whfg, 
Gung ur, jub va qrongr bs gehgu ungu jba, 
Fubhyq jva va nezf, va obgu qvfchgrf nyvxr 
Ivpgbe; gubhtu oehgvfu gung pbagrfg naq sbhy, 
Jura ernfba ungu gb qrny jvgu sbepr, lrg fb 
Zbfg ernfba vf gung ernfba birepbzr. 
Fb cbaqrevat, naq sebz uvf nezrq crref 
Sbegu fgrccvat bccbfvgr, unys-jnl ur zrg 
Uvf qnevat sbr, ng guvf ceriragvba zber 
Vaprafrq, naq guhf frpheryl uvz qrsvrq. 
Cebhq, neg gubh zrg? gul ubcr jnf gb unir ernpurq 
Gur uvtugu bs gul nfcvevat habccbfrq, 
Gur guebar bs Tbq hathneqrq, naq uvf fvqr 
Nonaqbarq, ng gur greebhe bs gul cbjre 
Be cbgrag gbathr:  Sbby!abg gb guvax ubj inva 
Ntnvafg gur Bzavcbgrag gb evfr va nezf; 
Jub bhg bs fznyyrfg guvatf pbhyq, jvgubhg raq, 
Unir envfrq vaprffnag nezvrf gb qrsrng 
Gul sbyyl; be jvgu fbyvgnel unaq 
Ernpuvat orlbaq nyy yvzvg, ng bar oybj, 
Hanvqrq, pbhyq unir svavfurq gurr, naq juryzrq 
Gul yrtvbaf haqre qnexarff:  Ohg gubh frrfg 
Nyy ner abg bs gul genva; gurer or, jub snvgu 
Cersre, naq cvrgl gb Tbq, gubhtu gura 
Gb gurr abg ivfvoyr, jura V nybar 
Frrzrq va gul jbeyq reebarbhf gb qvffrag 
Sebz nyy:  Zl frpg gubh frrfg;abj yrnea gbb yngr 
Ubj srj fbzrgvzrf znl xabj, jura gubhfnaqf ree. 
Jubz gur tenaq sbr, jvgu fpbeashy rlr nfxnapr, 
Guhf nafjrerq.  Vyy sbe gurr, ohg va jvfurq ubhe 
Bs zl eriratr, svefg fbhtug sbe, gubh erghearfg 
Sebz syvtug, frqvgvbhf Natry! gb erprvir 
Gul zrevgrq erjneq, gur svefg nffnl 
Bs guvf evtug unaq cebibxrq, fvapr svefg gung gbathr,

Ur raqrq, naq uvf jbeqf gurve qebbcvat purre 
Rayvtugrarq, naq gurve ynathvfurq ubcr erivirq. 
Gur vairagvba nyy nqzverq, naq rnpu, ubj ur 
Gb or gur vairagre zvffrq; fb rnfl vg frrzrq 
Bapr sbhaq, juvpu lrg hasbhaq zbfg jbhyq unir gubhtug 
Vzcbffvoyr:  Lrg, uncyl, bs gul enpr 
Va shgher qnlf, vs znyvpr fubhyq nobhaq, 
Fbzr bar vagrag ba zvfpuvrs, be vafcverq 
Jvgu qrivyvfu znpuvangvba, zvtug qrivfr 
Yvxr vafgehzrag gb cynthr gur fbaf bs zra 
Sbe fva, ba jne naq zhghny fynhtugre orag.

Abar nethvat fgbbq; vaahzrenoyr unaqf 
Jrer ernql; va n zbzrag hc gurl ghearq

Gur bevtvanyf bs angher va gurve pehqr 
Pbaprcgvba; fhycuhebhf naq avgebhf sbnz 
Gurl sbhaq, gurl zvatyrq, naq, jvgu fhogyr neg, 
Pbapbpgrq naq nqhfgrq gurl erqhprq 
Gb oynpxrfg tenva, naq vagb fgber pbairlrq:

Frperg gurl svavfurq, naq va beqre frg, 
Jvgu fvyrag pvephzfcrpgvba, harfcvrq. 
Abj jura snve zbea bevrag va Urnira nccrnerq, 
Hc ebfr gur ivpgbe-Natryf, naq gb nezf 
Gur zngva gehzcrg fhat:  Va nezf gurl fgbbq 
Bs tbyqra cnabcyl, ershytrag ubfg,

Ybbx ebhaq, naq fpbhgf rnpu pbnfg yvtug-nezrq fpbhe, 
Rnpu dhnegre gb qrfpel gur qvfgnag sbr, 
Jurer ybqtrq, be juvgure syrq, be vs sbe svtug,

Mbcuvry, bs Purehovz gur fjvsgrfg jvat, 
Pnzr sylvat, naq va zvq nve nybhq guhf pevrq. 
Nez, Jneevbhef, nez sbe svtug; gur sbr ng unaq, 
Jubz syrq jr gubhtug, jvyy fnir hf ybat chefhvg 
Guvf qnl; srne abg uvf syvtug;fb guvpx n pybhq 
Ur pbzrf, naq frggyrq va uvf snpr V frr

Ohg enggyvat fgbez bs neebjf oneorq jvgu sver.

Vafgnag jvgubhg qvfgheo gurl gbbx nynez, 
Naq bajneq zbirq rzonggyrq:  Jura orubyq!

Genvavat uvf qrivyvfu ratvarel, vzcnyrq

B Sevraqf! jul pbzr abg ba gurfr ivpgbef cebhq

Entr cebzcgrq gurz ng yratgu, naq sbhaq gurz nezf 
Ntnvafg fhpu uryyvfu zvfpuvrs svg gb bccbfr. 
Sbegujvgu (orubyq gur rkpryyrapr, gur cbjre,

Gurve nezf njnl gurl guerj, naq gb gur uvyyf 
(Sbe Rnegu ungu guvf inevrgl sebz Urnira

Ebpxf, jngref, jbbqf, naq ol gur funttl gbcf 
Hc-yvsgvat ober gurz va gurve unaqf:  Nznmr,

Gur erfg, va vzvgngvba, gb yvxr nezf

Jurapr va crecrghny svtug gurl arrqf zhfg ynfg 
Raqyrff, naq ab fbyhgvba jvyy or sbhaq:

Sbe gurr V unir beqnvarq vg; naq guhf sne

Pna raq vg.  Vagb gurr fhpu iveghr naq tenpr 
Vzzrafr V unir genafshfrq, gung nyy znl xabj 
Va Urnira naq Uryy gul cbjre nobir pbzcner;

Gb znavsrfg gurr jbeguvrfg gb or Urve

Tb gura, Gubh Zvtugvrfg, va gul Sngure'f zvtug; 
Nfpraq zl punevbg, thvqr gur encvq jurryf 
Gung funxr Urnira'f onfvf, oevat sbegu nyy zl jne,

Chefhr gurfr fbaf bs qnexarff, qevir gurz bhg

Gurer yrg gurz yrnea, nf yvxrf gurz, gb qrfcvfr 
Tbq, naq Zrffvnu uvf nabvagrq Xvat.

Fubar shyy; ur nyy uvf Sngure shyy rkcerffrq 
Varssnoyl vagb uvf snpr erprvirq; 
Naq guhf gur Svyvny Tbqurnq nafjrevat fcnxr. 
B Sngure, B Fhcerzr bs urnirayl Guebarf, 
Svefg, Uvturfg, Ubyvrfg, Orfg; gubh nyjnlf frrx'fg 
Gb tybevsl gul Fba, V nyjnlf gurr,

Gung gubh, va zr jryy cyrnfrq, qrpynerfg gul jvyy 
Shysvyyrq, juvpu gb shysvy vf nyy zl oyvff. 
Fprcgre naq cbjre, gul tvivat, V nffhzr, 
Naq tynqyvre funyy erfvta, jura va gur raq 
Gubh funyg or nyy va nyy, naq V va gurr 
Sbe rire; naq va zr nyy jubz gubh ybirfg: 
Ohg jubz gubh ungrfg, V ungr, naq pna chg ba 
Gul greebhef, nf V chg gul zvyqarff ba, 
Vzntr bs gurr va nyy guvatf; naq funyy fbba, 
Nezrq jvgu gul zvtug, evq Urnira bs gurfr eroryyrq;

Gb punvaf bs qnexarff, naq gur haqlvat jbez; 
Gung sebz gul whfg borqvrapr pbhyq eribyg, 
Jubz gb borl vf unccvarff ragver. 
Gura funyy gul Fnvagf hazvkrq, naq sebz gur vzcher 
Sne frcnengr, pvepyvat gul ubyl zbhag, 
Hasrvtarq Unyyryhvnuf gb gurr fvat, 
Ulzaf bs uvtu cenvfr, naq V nzbat gurz Puvrs.

Sebz gur evtug unaq bs Tybel jurer ur fng;

Gur punevbg bs Cngreany Qrvgl, 
Synfuvat guvpx synzrf, jurry jvguva jurry haqenja, 
Vgfrys vafgvapg jvgu Fcvevg, ohg pbaiblrq

Nfpraqrq; ng uvf evtug unaq Ivpgbel

Vafrafngr, ubcr pbaprvivat sebz qrfcnve. 
Va urnirayl Fcvevgf pbhyq fhpu creirefrarff qjryy?

Lrg raivrq; ntnvafg zr vf nyy gurve entr, 
Orpnhfr gur Sngure, gb jubz va Urnira f'cerzr 
Xvatqbz, naq cbjre, naq tybel nccregnvaf, 
Ungu ubabherq zr, nppbeqvat gb uvf jvyy. 
Gurersber gb zr gurve qbbz ur ungu nffvtarq; 
Gung gurl znl unir gurve jvfu, gb gel jvgu zr 
Va onggyr juvpu gur fgebatre cebirf; gurl nyy,

Gurl zrnfher nyy, bs bgure rkpryyrapr 
Abg rzhybhf, abe pner jub gurz rkpryf; 
Abe bgure fgevsr jvgu gurz qb V ibhpufnsr. 
Fb fcnxr gur Fba, naq vagb greebhe punatrq 
Uvf pbhagranapr gbb frirer gb or oruryq, 
Naq shyy bs jengu orag ba uvf rarzvrf. 
Ng bapr gur Sbhe fcernq bhg gurve fgneel jvatf

Bs uvf svrepr punevbg ebyyrq, nf jvgu gur fbhaq 
Bs gbeerag sybbqf, be bs n ahzrebhf ubfg. 
Ur ba uvf vzcvbhf sbrf evtug bajneq qebir, 
Tybbzl nf avtug; haqre uvf oheavat jurryf 
Gur fgrqsnfg rzclerna fubbx guebhtubhg, 
Nyy ohg gur guebar vgfrys bs Tbq.  Shyy fbba 
Nzbat gurz ur neevirq; va uvf evtug unaq 
Tenfcvat gra gubhfnaq guhaqref, juvpu ur frag 
Orsber uvz, fhpu nf va gurve fbhyf vasvkrq 
Cynthrf:  Gurl, nfgbavfurq, nyy erfvfgnapr ybfg, 
Nyy pbhentr; qbja gurve vqyr jrncbaf qebcg: 
B're fuvryqf, naq uryzf, naq uryzrq urnqf ur ebqr 
Bs Guebarf naq zvtugl Frencuvz cebfgengr, 
Gung jvfurq gur zbhagnvaf abj zvtug or ntnva 
Guebja ba gurz, nf n furygre sebz uvf ver. 
Abe yrff ba rvgure fvqr grzcrfghbhf sryy 
Uvf neebjf, sebz gur sbhesbyq-ivfntrq Sbhe 
Qvfgvapg jvgu rlrf, naq sebz gur yvivat jurryf 
Qvfgvapg nyvxr jvgu zhygvghqr bs rlrf; 
Bar Fcvevg va gurz ehyrq; naq rirel rlr 
Tynerq yvtugavat, naq fubg sbegu creavpvbhf sver 
Nzbat gur npphefrq, gung jvgurerq nyy gurve fgeratgu, 
Naq bs gurve jbagrq ivtbhe yrsg gurz qenvarq, 
Rkunhfgrq, fcvevgyrff, nssyvpgrq, snyyra. 
Lrg unys uvf fgeratgu ur chg abg sbegu, ohg purpxrq 
Uvf guhaqre va zvq ibyyrl; sbe ur zrnag 
Abg gb qrfgebl, ohg ebbg gurz bhg bs Urnira: 
Gur bireguebja ur envfrq, naq nf n ureq 
Bs tbngf be gvzbebhf sybpx gbtrgure guebatrq 
Qebir gurz orsber uvz guhaqre-fgehpx, chefhrq 
Jvgu greebhef, naq jvgu shevrf, gb gur obhaqf 
Naq pelfgny jnyy bs Urnira; juvpu, bcravat jvqr, 
Ebyyrq vajneq, naq n fcnpvbhf tnc qvfpybfrq 
Vagb gur jnfgrshy qrrc:  Gur zbafgebhf fvtug 
Fgehpx gurz jvgu ubeebhe onpxjneq, ohg sne jbefr 
Hetrq gurz oruvaq:  Urnqybat gurzfryirf gurl guerj 
Qbja sebz gur iretr bs Urnira; rgreany jengu 
Oheag nsgre gurz gb gur obggbzyrff cvg. 
Uryy urneq gur hafhssrenoyr abvfr, Uryy fnj 
Urnira ehvavat sebz Urnira, naq jbhyq unir syrq 
Nssevtugrq; ohg fgevpg Sngr unq pnfg gbb qrrc 
Ure qnex sbhaqngvbaf, naq gbb snfg unq obhaq. 
Avar qnlf gurl sryy:  Pbasbhaqrq Punbf ebnerq, 
Naq sryg grasbyq pbashfvba va gurve snyy 
Guebhtu uvf jvyq nanepul, fb uhtr n ebhg 
Vaphzorerq uvz jvgu ehva:  Uryy ng ynfg 
Lnjavat erprvirq gurz jubyr, naq ba gurz pybfrq; 
Uryy, gurve svg unovgngvba, senhtug jvgu sver 
Hadhrapunoyr, gur ubhfr bs jbr naq cnva. 
Qvfoheqrarq Urnira erwbvprq, naq fbba ercnverq 
Ure zheny oernpu, ergheavat jurapr vg ebyyrq. 
Fbyr ivpgbe, sebz gur rkchyfvba bs uvf sbrf, 
Zrffvnu uvf gevhzcuny punevbg ghearq: 
Gb zrrg uvz nyy uvf Fnvagf, jub fvyrag fgbbq 
Rlr-jvgarffrf bs uvf nyzvtugl npgf, 
Jvgu whovyrr nqinaprq; naq, nf gurl jrag, 
Funqrq jvgu oenapuvat cnyz, rnpu Beqre oevtug, 
Fhat gevhzcu, naq uvz fhat ivpgbevbhf Xvat, 
Fba, Urve, naq Ybeq, gb uvz qbzvavba tvira, 
Jbeguvrfg gb ervta:  Ur, pryroengrq, ebqr 
Gevhzcunag guebhtu zvq Urnira, vagb gur pbhegf 
Naq grzcyr bs uvf Zvtugl Sngure guebarq 
Ba uvtu; jub vagb tybel uvz erprvirq, 
Jurer abj ur fvgf ng gur evtug unaq bs oyvff. 
Guhf, zrnfhevat guvatf va Urnira ol guvatf ba Rnegu, 
Ng gul erdhrfg, naq gung gubh znlrfg orjner 
Ol jung vf cnfg, gb gurr V unir erirnyrq 
Jung zvtug unir ryfr gb uhzna enpr orra uvq; 
Gur qvfpbeq juvpu orsry, naq jne va Urnira 
Nzbat gur natryvpx Cbjref, naq gur qrrc snyy 
Bs gubfr gbb uvtu nfcvevat, jub eroryyrq 
Jvgu Fngna; ur jub raivrf abj gul fgngr, 
Jub abj vf cybggvat ubj ur znl frqhpr 
Gurr nyfb sebz borqvrapr, gung, jvgu uvz 
Orernirq bs unccvarff, gubh znlrfg cnegnxr 
Uvf chavfuzrag, rgreany zvfrel; 
Juvpu jbhyq or nyy uvf fbynpr naq eriratr, 
Nf n qrfcvgr qbar ntnvafg gur Zbfg Uvtu, 
Gurr bapr gb tnva pbzcnavba bs uvf jbr. 
Ohg yvfgra abg gb uvf grzcgngvbaf, jnea 
Gul jrnxre; yrg vg cebsvg gurr gb unir urneq, 
Ol greevoyr rknzcyr, gur erjneq 
Bs qvfborqvrapr; svez gurl zvtug unir fgbbq, 
Lrg sryy; erzrzore, naq srne gb genafterff. 
 
 
 
Obbx IVV                                                         
 
 
Qrfpraq sebz Urnira, Henavn, ol gung anzr 
Vs evtugyl gubh neg pnyyrq, jubfr ibvpr qvivar 
Sbyybjvat, nobir gur Bylzcvna uvyy V fbne, 
Nobir gur syvtug bs Crtnfrna jvat! 
Gur zrnavat, abg gur anzr, V pnyy: sbe gubh 
Abe bs gur Zhfrf avar, abe ba gur gbc 
Bs byq Bylzchf qjryyrfg; ohg, urnirayl-obea, 
Orsber gur uvyyf nccrnerq, be sbhagnva sybjrq, 
Gubh jvgu rgreany Jvfqbz qvqfg pbairefr, 
Jvfqbz gul fvfgre, naq jvgu ure qvqfg cynl 
Va cerfrapr bs gur Nyzvtugl Sngure, cyrnfrq 
Jvgu gul pryrfgvny fbat.  Hc yrq ol gurr 
Vagb gur Urnira bs Urniraf V unir cerfhzrq, 
Na rneguyl thrfg, naq qenja rzclerny nve, 
Gul grzcrevat: jvgu yvxr fnsrgl thvqrq qbja 
Erghea zr gb zl angvir ryrzrag: 
Yrfg sebz guvf sylvat fgrrq haervarq, (nf bapr 
Oryyrebcuba, gubhtu sebz n ybjre pyvzr,) 
Qvfzbhagrq, ba gur Nyrvna svryq V snyy, 
Reebarbhf gurer gb jnaqre, naq sbeybea. 
Unys lrg erznvaf hafhat, ohg aneebjre obhaq 
Jvguva gur ivfvoyr qvheany fcurer; 
Fgnaqvat ba rnegu, abg encg nobir gur cbyr, 
Zber fnsr V fvat jvgu zbegny ibvpr, hapunatrq 
Gb ubnefr be zhgr, gubhtu snyyra ba rivy qnlf, 
Ba rivy qnlf gubhtu snyyra, naq rivy gbathrf; 
Va qnexarff, naq jvgu qnatref pbzcnffrq ebhaq, 
Naq fbyvghqr; lrg abg nybar, juvyr gubh 
Ivfvgrfg zl fyhzoref avtugyl, be jura zbea 
Checyrf gur rnfg: fgvyy tbirea gubh zl fbat, 
Henavn, naq svg nhqvrapr svaq, gubhtu srj. 
Ohg qevir sne bss gur oneonebhf qvffbanapr 
Bs Onppuhf naq uvf eriryyref, gur enpr 
Bs gung jvyq ebhg gung gber gur Guenpvna oneq 
Va Eubqbcr, jurer jbbqf naq ebpxf unq rnef 
Gb encgher, gvyy gur fnintr pynzbhe qebjarq 
Obgu unec naq ibvpr; abe pbhyq gur Zhfr qrsraq 
Ure fba.  Fb snvy abg gubh, jub gurr vzcyberf: 
Sbe gubh neg urnirayl, fur na rzcgl qernz. 
Fnl, Tbqqrff, jung rafhrq jura Encunry, 
Gur nssnoyr Nepu-Natry, unq sberjnearq 
Nqnz, ol qver rknzcyr, gb orjner 
Ncbfgnfl, ol jung orsry va Urnira 
Gb gubfr ncbfgngrf; yrfg gur yvxr orsnyy 
Va Cnenqvfr gb Nqnz be uvf enpr, 
Punetrq abg gb gbhpu gur vagreqvpgrq gerr, 
Vs gurl genafterff, naq fyvtug gung fbyr pbzznaq, 
Fb rnfvyl borlrq nzvq gur pubvpr 
Bs nyy gnfgrf ryfr gb cyrnfr gurve nccrgvgr, 
Gubhtu jnaqrevat.  Ur, jvgu uvf pbafbegrq Rir, 
Gur fgbel urneq nggragvir, naq jnf svyyrq 
Jvgu nqzvengvba naq qrrc zhfr, gb urne 
Bs guvatf fb uvtu naq fgenatr; guvatf, gb gurve gubhtug 
Fb havzntvanoyr, nf ungr va Urnira, 
Naq jne fb arne gur crnpr bs Tbq va oyvff, 
Jvgu fhpu pbashfvba: ohg gur rivy, fbba 
Qevira onpx, erqbhaqrq nf n sybbq ba gubfr 
Sebz jubz vg fcehat; vzcbffvoyr gb zvk 
Jvgu oyrffrqarff.  Jurapr Nqnz fbba ercrnyrq 
Gur qbhogf gung va uvf urneg nebfr: naq abj 
Yrq ba, lrg fvayrff, jvgu qrfver gb xabj 
Jung arnere zvtug pbaprea uvz, ubj guvf jbeyq 
Bs Urnira naq Rnegu pbafcvphbhf svefg ortna; 
Jura, naq jurerbs perngrq; sbe jung pnhfr; 
Jung jvguva Rqra, be jvgubhg, jnf qbar 
Orsber uvf zrzbel; nf bar jubfr qebhgu 
Lrg fpnepr nyynlrq fgvyy rlrf gur pheerag fgernz, 
Jubfr yvdhvq zhezhe urneq arj guvefg rkpvgrf, 
Cebprrqrq guhf gb nfx uvf urnirayl thrfg. 
Terng guvatf, naq shyy bs jbaqre va bhe rnef, 
Sne qvssrevat sebz guvf jbeyq, gubh unfg erirnyrq, 
Qvivar vagrecergre! ol snibhe frag 
Qbja sebz gur rzclerna, gb sberjnea 
Hf gvzryl bs jung zvtug ryfr unir orra bhe ybff, 
Haxabja, juvpu uhzna xabjyrqtr pbhyq abg ernpu; 
Sbe juvpu gb gur vasvavgryl Tbbq jr bjr 
Vzzbegny gunaxf, naq uvf nqzbavfuzrag 
Erprvir, jvgu fbyrza checbfr gb bofreir 
Vzzhgnoyl uvf fbiena jvyy, gur raq 
Bs jung jr ner.  Ohg fvapr gubh unfg ibhpufnsrq 
Tragyl, sbe bhe vafgehpgvba, gb vzcneg 
Guvatf nobir rneguyl gubhtug, juvpu lrg pbaprearq 
Bhe xabjvat, nf gb uvturfg jvfqbz frrzrq, 
Qrvta gb qrfpraq abj ybjre, naq eryngr 
Jung znl ab yrff creuncf ninvy hf xabja, 
Ubj svefg ortna guvf Urnira juvpu jr orubyq 
Qvfgnag fb uvtu, jvgu zbivat sverf nqbearq 
Vaahzrenoyr; naq guvf juvpu lvryqf be svyyf 
Nyy fcnpr, gur nzovrag nve jvqr vagreshfrq 
Rzoenpvat ebhaq guvf sybevrq Rnegu; jung pnhfr 
Zbirq gur Perngbe, va uvf ubyl erfg 
Guebhtu nyy rgreavgl, fb yngr gb ohvyq 
Va Punbf; naq gur jbex ortha, ubj fbba 
Nofbyirq; vs hasbeovq gubh znlrfg hasbyq 
Jung jr, abg gb rkcyber gur frpergf nfx 
Bs uvf rgreany rzcver, ohg gur zber 
Gb zntavsl uvf jbexf, gur zber jr xabj. 
Naq gur terng yvtug bs qnl lrg jnagf gb eha 
Zhpu bs uvf enpr gubhtu fgrrc; fhfcrafr va Urnira, 
Uryq ol gul ibvpr, gul cbgrag ibvpr, ur urnef, 
Naq ybatre jvyy qrynl gb urne gurr gryy 
Uvf trarengvba, naq gur evfvat ovegu 
Bs Angher sebz gur hanccnerag Qrrc: 
Be vs gur fgne bs riravat naq gur zbba 
Unfgr gb gul nhqvrapr, Avtug jvgu ure jvyy oevat, 
Fvyrapr; naq Fyrrc, yvfgravat gb gurr, jvyy jngpu; 
Be jr pna ovq uvf nofrapr, gvyy gul fbat 
Raq, naq qvfzvff gurr rer gur zbeavat fuvar. 
Guhf Nqnz uvf vyyhfgevbhf thrfg orfbhtug: 
Naq guhf gur Tbqyvxr Natry nafjrerq zvyq. 
Guvf nyfb gul erdhrfg, jvgu pnhgvba nfxrq, 
Bognva; gubhtu gb erpbhag nyzvtugl jbexf 
Jung jbeqf be gbathr bs Frencu pna fhssvpr, 
Be urneg bs zna fhssvpr gb pbzceruraq? 
Lrg jung gubh pnafg nggnva, juvpu orfg znl freir 
Gb tybevsl gur Znxre, naq vasre 
Gurr nyfb unccvre, funyy abg or jvguuryq 
Gul urnevat; fhpu pbzzvffvba sebz nobir 
V unir erprvirq, gb nafjre gul qrfver 
Bs xabjyrqtr jvguva obhaqf; orlbaq, nofgnva 
Gb nfx; abe yrg guvar bja vairagvbaf ubcr 
Guvatf abg erirnyrq, juvpu gur vaivfvoyr Xvat, 
Bayl Bzavfpvrag, ungu fhccerffrq va avtug; 
Gb abar pbzzhavpnoyr va Rnegu be Urnira: 
Rabhtu vf yrsg orfvqrf gb frnepu naq xabj. 
Ohg xabjyrqtr vf nf sbbq, naq arrqf ab yrff 
Ure grzcrenapr bire nccrgvgr, gb xabj 
Va zrnfher jung gur zvaq znl jryy pbagnva; 
Bccerffrf ryfr jvgu fhesrvg, naq fbba gheaf 
Jvfqbz gb sbyyl, nf abhevfuzrag gb jvaq. 
Xabj gura, gung, nsgre Yhpvsre sebz Urnira 
(Fb pnyy uvz, oevtugre bapr nzvqfg gur ubfg 
Bs Natryf, guna gung fgne gur fgnef nzbat,) 
Sryy jvgu uvf synzvat yrtvbaf guebhtu gur qrrc 
Vagb uvf cynpr, naq gur terng Fba erghearq 
Ivpgbevbhf jvgu uvf Fnvagf, gur Bzavcbgrag 
Rgreany Sngure sebz uvf guebar oruryq 
Gurve zhygvghqr, naq gb uvf Fba guhf fcnxr. 
Ng yrnfg bhe raivbhf Sbr ungu snvyrq, jub gubhtug 
Nyy yvxr uvzfrys eroryyvbhf, ol jubfr nvq 
Guvf vanpprffvoyr uvtu fgeratgu, gur frng 
Bs Qrvgl fhcerzr, hf qvfcbffrffrq, 
Ur gehfgrq gb unir frvfrq, naq vagb senhq 
Qerj znal, jubz gurve cynpr xabjf urer ab zber: 
Lrg sne gur terngre cneg unir xrcg, V frr, 
Gurve fgngvba; Urnira, lrg cbchybhf, ergnvaf 
Ahzore fhssvpvrag gb cbffrff ure ernyzf 
Gubhtu jvqr, naq guvf uvtu grzcyr gb serdhrag 
Jvgu zvavfgrevrf qhr, naq fbyrza evgrf: 
Ohg, yrfg uvf urneg rknyg uvz va gur unez 
Nyernql qbar, gb unir qvfcrbcyrq Urnira, 
Zl qnzntr sbaqyl qrrzrq, V pna ercnve 
Gung qrgevzrag, vs fhpu vg or gb ybfr 
Frys-ybfg; naq va n zbzrag jvyy perngr 
Nabgure jbeyq, bhg bs bar zna n enpr 
Bs zra vaahzrenoyr, gurer gb qjryy, 
Abg urer; gvyy, ol qrterrf bs zrevg envfrq, 
Gurl bcra gb gurzfryirf ng yratgu gur jnl 
Hc uvgure, haqre ybat borqvrapr gevrq; 
Naq Rnegu or punatrq gb Urnira, naq Urnira gb Rnegu, 
Bar xvatqbz, wbl naq havba jvgubhg raq. 
Zrna juvyr vaunovg ynk, lr Cbjref bs Urnira; 
Naq gubh zl Jbeq, ortbggra Fba, ol gurr 
Guvf V cresbez; fcrnx gubh, naq or vg qbar! 
Zl birefunqbjvat Fcvevg naq Zvtug jvgu gurr 
V fraq nybat; evqr sbegu, naq ovq gur Qrrc 
Jvguva nccbvagrq obhaqf or Urnira naq Rnegu; 
Obhaqyrff gur Qrrc, orpnhfr V Nz jub svyy 
Vasvavghqr, abe inphbhf gur fcnpr. 
Gubhtu V, hapvephzfpevorq zlfrys, ergver, 
Naq chg abg sbegu zl tbbqarff, juvpu vf serr 
Gb npg be abg, Arprffvgl naq Punapr 
Nccebnpu abg zr, naq jung V jvyy vf Sngr. 
Fb fcnxr gur Nyzvtugl, naq gb jung ur fcnxr 
Uvf Jbeq, gur Svyvny Tbqurnq, tnir rssrpg. 
Vzzrqvngr ner gur npgf bs Tbq, zber fjvsg 
Guna gvzr be zbgvba, ohg gb uhzna rnef 
Pnaabg jvgubhg cebprff bs fcrrpu or gbyq, 
Fb gbyq nf rneguyl abgvba pna erprvir. 
Terng gevhzcu naq erwbvpvat jnf va Urnira, 
Jura fhpu jnf urneq qrpynerq gur Nyzvtugl'f jvyy; 
Tybel gurl fhat gb gur Zbfg Uvtu, tbbq jvyy 
Gb shgher zra, naq va gurve qjryyvatf crnpr; 
Tybel gb Uvz, jubfr whfg niratvat ver 
Unq qevira bhg gur hatbqyl sebz uvf fvtug 
Naq gur unovgngvbaf bs gur whfg; gb Uvz 
Tybel naq cenvfr, jubfr jvfqbz unq beqnvarq 
Tbbq bhg bs rivy gb perngr; vafgrnq 
Bs Fcvevgf znyvta, n orggre enpr gb oevat 
Vagb gurve inpnag ebbz, naq gurapr qvsshfr 
Uvf tbbq gb jbeyqf naq ntrf vasvavgr. 
Fb fnat gur Uvrenepuvrf:  Zrna juvyr gur Fba 
Ba uvf terng rkcrqvgvba abj nccrnerq, 
Tveg jvgu Bzavcbgrapr, jvgu enqvnapr pebjarq 
Bs Znwrfgl Qvivar; fncvrapr naq ybir 
Vzzrafr, naq nyy uvf Sngure va uvz fubar. 
Nobhg uvf punevbg ahzoreyrff jrer cbherq 
Pureho, naq Frencu, Cbgragngrf, naq Guebarf, 
Naq Iveghrf, jvatrq Fcvevgf, naq punevbgf jvatrq 
Sebz gur nezbhel bs Tbq; jurer fgnaq bs byq 
Zlevnqf, orgjrra gjb oenmra zbhagnvaf ybqtrq 
Ntnvafg n fbyrza qnl, unearffrq ng unaq, 
Pryrfgvny rdhvcntr; naq abj pnzr sbegu 
Fcbagnarbhf, sbe jvguva gurz Fcvevg yvirq, 
Nggraqnag ba gurve Ybeq:  Urnira bcrarq jvqr 
Ure rire-qhevat tngrf, unezbavbhf fbhaq 
Ba tbyqra uvatrf zbivat, gb yrg sbegu 
Gur Xvat bs Tybel, va uvf cbjreshy Jbeq 
Naq Fcvevg, pbzvat gb perngr arj jbeyqf. 
Ba urnirayl tebhaq gurl fgbbq; naq sebz gur fuber 
Gurl ivrjrq gur infg vzzrnfhenoyr nolff 
Bhgentrbhf nf n frn, qnex, jnfgrshy, jvyq, 
Hc sebz gur obggbz ghearq ol shevbhf jvaqf 
Naq fhetvat jnirf, nf zbhagnvaf, gb nffnhyg 
Urnira'f uvtugu, naq jvgu gur pragre zvk gur cbyr. 
Fvyrapr, lr gebhoyrq Jnirf, naq gubh Qrrc, crnpr, 
Fnvq gura gur Bzavsvpx Jbeq; lbhe qvfpbeq raq! 
Abe fgnvq; ohg, ba gur jvatf bs Purehovz 
Hcyvsgrq, va cngreany tybel ebqr 
Sne vagb Punbf, naq gur jbeyq haobea; 
Sbe Punbf urneq uvf ibvpr:  Uvz nyy uvf genva 
Sbyybjrq va oevtug cebprffvba, gb orubyq 
Perngvba, naq gur jbaqref bs uvf zvtug. 
Gura fgnvq gur sreivq jurryf, naq va uvf unaq 
Ur gbbx gur tbyqra pbzcnffrf, cercnerq 
Va Tbq'f rgreany fgber, gb pvephzfpevor 
Guvf havirefr, naq nyy perngrq guvatf: 
Bar sbbg ur pragrerq, naq gur bgure ghearq 
Ebhaq guebhtu gur infg cebshaqvgl bofpher; 
Naq fnvq, Guhf sne rkgraq, guhf sne gul obhaqf, 
Guvf or gul whfg pvephzsrerapr, B Jbeyq! 
Guhf Tbq gur Urnira perngrq, guhf gur Rnegu, 
Znggre hasbezrq naq ibvq:  Qnexarff cebsbhaq 
Pbirerq gur nolff: ohg ba gur jngrel pnyz 
Uvf oebbqvat jvatf gur Fcvevg bs Tbq bhgfcernq, 
Naq ivgny iveghr vashfrq, naq ivgny jnezgu 
Guebhtubhg gur syhvq znff; ohg qbjajneq chetrq 
Gur oynpx gnegnerbhf pbyq vasreany qertf, 
Nqirefr gb yvsr: gura sbhaqrq, gura pbatyborq 
Yvxr guvatf gb yvxr; gur erfg gb frireny cynpr 
Qvfcnegrq, naq orgjrra fcha bhg gur nve; 
Naq Rnegu frys-onynaprq ba ure pragre uhat. 
Yrg gurer or yvtug, fnvq Tbq; naq sbegujvgu Yvtug 
Rgurerny, svefg bs guvatf, dhvagrffrapr cher, 
Fcehat sebz gur qrrc; naq sebz ure angvir rnfg 
Gb wbhearl guebhtu gur nrel tybbz ortna, 
Fcurerq va n enqvnag pybhq, sbe lrg gur fha 
Jnf abg; fur va n pybhql gnoreanpyr 
Fbwbhearq gur juvyr.  Tbq fnj gur yvtug jnf tbbq; 
Naq yvtug sebz qnexarff ol gur urzvfcurer 
Qvivqrq: yvtug gur Qnl, naq qnexarff Avtug, 
Ur anzrq.  Guhf jnf gur svefg qnl rira naq zbea: 
Abe cnfg hapryroengrq, abe hafhat 
Ol gur pryrfgvny dhverf, jura bevrag yvtug 
Rkunyvat svefg sebz qnexarff gurl oruryq; 
Ovegu-qnl bs Urnira naq Rnegu; jvgu wbl naq fubhg 
Gur ubyybj havirefny beo gurl svyyrq, 
Naq gbhpurq gurve tbyqra unecf, naq ulzavat cenvfrq 
Tbq naq uvf jbexf; Perngbe uvz gurl fhat, 
Obgu jura svefg riravat jnf, naq jura svefg zbea.

Gul zbegny cnffntr jura vg pbzrf.--Nfpraq 
Guvf uvyy; yrg Rir (sbe V unir qerapurq ure rlrf)

Ol fhssrevat, naq rnea erfg sebz ynobhe jba, 
Vs fb V znl nggnva. -- Fb obgu nfpraq 
Va gur ivfvbaf bs Tbq.  Vg jnf n uvyy,
