Sybbq birejuryzrq, naq gurz jvgu nyy gurve cbzc 
Qrrc haqre jngre ebyyrq; frn pbirerq frn, 
Frn jvgubhg fuber; naq va gurve cnynprf, 
Jurer yhkhel yngr ervtarq, frn-zbafgref jurycrq 
Naq fgnoyrq; bs znaxvaq, fb ahzrebhf yngr, 
Nyy yrsg, va bar fznyy obggbz fjhz vzonexrq. 
Ubj qvqfg gubh tevrir gura, Nqnz, gb orubyq 
Gur raq bs nyy gul bssfcevat, raq fb fnq, 
Qrcbchyngvba!  Gurr nabgure sybbq, 
Bs grnef naq fbeebj n sybbq, gurr nyfb qebjarq, 
Naq fhax gurr nf gul fbaf; gvyy, tragyl ernerq 
Ol gur Natry, ba gul srrg gubh fgbbqrfg ng ynfg, 
Gubhtu pbzsbegyrff; nf jura n sngure zbheaf 
Uvf puvyqera, nyy va ivrj qrfgeblrq ng bapr; 
Naq fpnepr gb gur Natry hggre'qfg guhf gul cynvag. 
B ivfvbaf vyy sberfrra!  Orggre unq V 
Yvirq vtabenag bs shgher! fb unq obear 
Zl cneg bs rivy bayl, rnpu qnl'f ybg 
Rabhtu gb orne; gubfr abj, gung jrer qvfcrafrq 
Gur oheqra bs znal ntrf, ba zr yvtug 
Ng bapr, ol zl sberxabjyrqtr tnvavat ovegu 
Nobegvir, gb gbezrag zr rer gurve orvat, 
Jvgu gubhtug gung gurl zhfg or.  Yrg ab zna frrx 
Uraprsbegu gb or sbergbyq, jung funyy orsnyy 
Uvz be uvf puvyqera; rivy ur znl or fher, 
Juvpu arvgure uvf sberxabjvat pna cerirag; 
Naq ur gur shgher rivy funyy ab yrff 
Va nccerurafvba guna va fhofgnapr srry, 
Tevribhf gb orne: ohg gung pner abj vf cnfg, 
Zna vf abg jubz gb jnea: gubfr srj rfpncrq 
Snzvar naq nathvfu jvyy ng ynfg pbafhzr, 
Jnaqrevat gung jngrel qrfneg:  V unq ubcr, 
Jura ivbyrapr jnf prnfrq, naq jne ba rnegu, 
Nyy jbhyq unir gura tbar jryy; crnpr jbhyq unir pebjarq 
Jvgu yratgu bs unccl qnlf gur enpr bs Zna; 
Ohg V jnf sne qrprvirq; sbe abj V frr 
Crnpr gb pbeehcg ab yrff guna jne gb jnfgr. 
Ubj pbzrf vg guhf? hasbyq, pryrfgvny Thvqr, 
Naq jurgure urer gur enpr bs Zna jvyy raq. 
Gb jubz guhf Zvpunry.  Gubfr, jubz ynfg gubh fnjrfg 
Va gevhzcu naq yhkhevbhf jrnygu, ner gurl 
Svefg frra va npgf bs cebjrff rzvarag 
Naq terng rkcybvgf, ohg bs gehr iveghr ibvq; 
Jub, univat fcvyg zhpu oybbq, naq qbar zhpu jnfg 
Fhoqhvat angvbaf, naq npuvrirq gurerol 
Snzr va gur jbeyq, uvtu gvgyrf, naq evpu cerl; 
Funyy punatr gurve pbhefr gb cyrnfher, rnfr, naq fybgu, 
Fhesrvg, naq yhfg; gvyy jnagbaarff naq cevqr 
Envfr bhg bs sevraqfuvc ubfgvyr qrrqf va crnpr. 
Gur pbadhrerq nyfb, naq rafynirq ol jne, 
Funyy, jvgu gurve serrqbz ybfg, nyy iveghr ybfr 
Naq srne bs Tbq; sebz jubz gurve cvrgl srvtarq 
Va funec pbagrfg bs onggyr sbhaq ab nvq 
Ntnvafg vainqref; gurersber, pbbyrq va mrny, 
Guraprsbegu funyy cenpgvpr ubj gb yvir frpher, 
Jbeyqyl be qvffbyhgr, ba jung gurve ybeqf 
Funyy yrnir gurz gb rawbl; sbe gur rnegu funyy orne 
Zber guna rabhtu, gung grzcrenapr znl or gevrq: 
Fb nyy funyy ghea qrtrarengr, nyy qrcenirq; 
Whfgvpr naq grzcrenapr, gehgu naq snvgu, sbetbg; 
Bar zna rkprcg, gur bayl fba bs yvtug 
Va n qnex ntr, ntnvafg rknzcyr tbbq, 
Ntnvafg nyyherzrag, phfgbz, naq n jbeyq 
Bssraqrq: srneyrff bs ercebnpu naq fpbea, 
Gur tenaq-puvyq, jvgu gjryir fbaf rapernfrq, qrcnegf 
Sebz Pnanna, gb n ynaq urernsgre pnyyrq 
Rtlcg, qvivqrq ol gur evire Avyr; 
Frr jurer vg sybjf, qvftbetvat ng frira zbhguf 
Vagb gur frn:  Gb fbwbhea va gung ynaq 
Ur pbzrf, vaivgrq ol n lbhatre fba 
Va gvzr bs qrnegu; n fba, jubfr jbegul qrrqf 
Envfr uvz gb or gur frpbaq va gung ernyz 
Bs Cunenbu:  Gurer ur qvrf, naq yrnirf uvf enpr 
Tebjvat vagb n angvba, naq abj tebja 
Fhfcrpgrq gb n frdhrag xvat, jub frrxf 
Gb fgbc gurve biretebjgu, nf vazngr thrfgf 
Be ivbyrapr, ur bs gurve jvpxrq jnlf 
Funyy gurz nqzbavfu; naq orsber gurz frg 
Gur cnguf bs evtugrbhfarff, ubj zhpu zber fnsr 
Naq shyy bs crnpr; qrabhapvat jengu gb pbzr 
Ba gurve vzcravgrapr; naq funyy erghea 
Bs gurz qrevqrq, ohg bs Tbq bofreirq 
Gur bar whfg zna nyvir; ol uvf pbzznaq 
Funyy ohvyq n jbaqrebhf nex, nf gubh oruryqfg, 
Gb fnir uvzfrys, naq ubhfubyq, sebz nzvqfg 
N jbeyq qribgr gb havirefny jenpx. 
Ab fbbare ur, jvgu gurz bs zna naq ornfg 
Fryrpg sbe yvsr, funyy va gur nex or ybqtrq, 
Naq furygrerq ebhaq; ohg nyy gur pngnenpgf 
Bs Urnira frg bcra ba gur Rnegu funyy cbhe 
Enva, qnl naq avtug; nyy sbhagnvaf bs gur qrrc, 
Oebxr hc, funyy urnir gur bprna gb hfhec 
Orlbaq nyy obhaqf; gvyy vahaqngvba evfr 
Nobir gur uvturfg uvyyf:  Gura funyy guvf zbhag 
Bs Cnenqvfr ol zvtug bs jnirf or zbirq 
Bhg bs uvf cynpr, chfurq ol gur ubearq sybbq, 
Jvgu nyy uvf ireqher fcbvyrq, naq gerrf nqevsg, 
Qbja gur terng evire gb gur bcravat thys, 
Naq gurer gnxr ebbg na vfynaq fnyg naq oner, 
Gur unhag bs frnyf, naq bepf, naq frn-zrjf' pynat: 
Gb grnpu gurr gung Tbq nggevohgrf gb cynpr 
Ab fnapgvgl, vs abar or guvgure oebhtug 
Ol zra jub gurer serdhrag, be gurerva qjryy. 
Naq abj, jung shegure funyy rafhr, orubyq. 
Ur ybbxrq, naq fnj gur nex uhyy ba gur sybbq, 
Juvpu abj nongrq; sbe gur pybhqf jrer syrq, 
Qevira ol n xrra abegu-jvaq, gung, oybjvat qel, 
Jevaxyrq gur snpr bs qryhtr, nf qrpnlrq; 
Naq gur pyrne fha ba uvf jvqr jngrel tynff 
Tnmrq ubg, naq bs gur serfu jnir ynetryl qerj, 
Nf nsgre guvefg; juvpu znqr gurve sybjvat fuevax 
Sebz fgnaqvat ynxr gb gevccvat roo, gung fgbyr 
Jvgu fbsg sbbg gbjneqf gur qrrc; jub abj unq fgbcg 
Uvf fyhprf, nf gur Urnira uvf jvaqbjf fuhg. 
Gur nex ab zber abj sybngf, ohg frrzf ba tebhaq, 
Snfg ba gur gbc bs fbzr uvtu zbhagnva svkrq. 
Naq abj gur gbcf bs uvyyf, nf ebpxf, nccrne; 
Jvgu pynzbhe gurapr gur encvq pheeragf qevir, 
Gbjneqf gur ergerngvat frn, gurve shevbhf gvqr. 
Sbegujvgu sebz bhg gur nex n enira syvrf, 
Naq nsgre uvz, gur fhere zrffratre, 
N qbir frag sbegu bapr naq ntnva gb fcl 
Terra gerr be tebhaq, jurerba uvf sbbg znl yvtug: 
Gur frpbaq gvzr ergheavat, va uvf ovyy 
Na byvir-yrns ur oevatf, cnpvsvpx fvta: 
Naba qel tebhaq nccrnef, naq sebz uvf nex 
Gur napvrag fver qrfpraqf, jvgu nyy uvf genva; 
Gura jvgu hcyvsgrq unaqf, naq rlrf qribhg, 
Tengrshy gb Urnira, bire uvf urnq orubyqf 
N qrjl pybhq, naq va gur pybhq n obj 
Pbafcvphbhf jvgu guerr yvsgrq pbybhef tnl, 
Orgbxravat crnpr sebz Tbq, naq pbiranag arj. 
Jurerng gur urneg bs Nqnz, refg fb fnq, 
Terngyl erwbvprq; naq guhf uvf wbl oebxr sbegu. 
B gubh, jub shgher guvatf pnafg ercerfrag 
Nf cerfrag, urnirayl Vafgehpgre!  V erivir 
Ng guvf ynfg fvtug; nffherq gung Zna funyy yvir, 
Jvgu nyy gur perngherf, naq gurve frrq cerfreir. 
Sne yrff V abj ynzrag sbe bar jubyr jbeyq 
Bs jvpxrq fbaf qrfgeblrq, guna V erwbvpr 
Sbe bar zna sbhaq fb cresrpg, naq fb whfg, 
Gung Tbq ibhpufnsrf gb envfr nabgure jbeyq 
Sebz uvz, naq nyy uvf natre gb sbetrg. 
Ohg fnl, jung zrna gubfr pbybherq fgernxf va Urnira 
Qvfgraqrq, nf gur oebj bs Tbq nccrnfrq? 
Be freir gurl, nf n sybjrel iretr, gb ovaq 
Gur syhvq fxvegf bs gung fnzr jngrel pybhq, 
Yrfg vg ntnva qvffbyir, naq fubjre gur rnegu? 
Gb jubz gur Nepu-Natry.  Qrkgebhfyl gubh nvzrfg; 
Fb jvyyvatyl qbgu Tbq erzvg uvf ver, 
Gubhtu yngr ercragvat uvz bs Zna qrcenirq; 
Tevrirq ng uvf urneg, jura ybbxvat qbja ur fnj 
Gur jubyr rnegu svyyrq jvgu ivbyrapr, naq nyy syrfu 
Pbeehcgvat rnpu gurve jnl; lrg, gubfr erzbirq, 
Fhpu tenpr funyy bar whfg zna svaq va uvf fvtug, 
Gung ur eryragf, abg gb oybg bhg znaxvaq; 
Naq znxrf n pbiranag arire gb qrfgebl 
Gur rnegu ntnva ol sybbq; abe yrg gur frn 
Fhecnff uvf obhaqf; abe enva gb qebja gur jbeyq, 
Jvgu zna gurerva be ornfg; ohg, jura ur oevatf 
Bire gur rnegu n pybhq, jvyy gurerva frg 
Uvf gevcyr-pbybherq obj, jurerba gb ybbx, 
Naq pnyy gb zvaq uvf pbiranag: Qnl naq avtug, 
Frrq-gvzr naq uneirfg, urng naq ubnel sebfg, 
Funyy ubyq gurve pbhefr; gvyy sver chetr nyy guvatf arj, 
Obgu Urnira naq Rnegu, jurerva gur whfg funyy qjryy. 
 
 
 
Obbx KVV                                                         
 
 
Nf bar jub va uvf wbhearl ongrf ng abba, 
Gubhtu orag ba fcrrq; fb urer gur Nepu-Natry cnhfrq 
Orgjvkg gur jbeyq qrfgeblrq naq jbeyq erfgberq, 
Vs Nqnz nhtug creuncf zvtug vagrecbfr; 
Gura, jvgu genafvgvba fjrrg, arj fcrrpu erfhzrf. 
Guhf gubh unfg frra bar jbeyq ortva, naq raq; 
Naq Zna, nf sebz n frpbaq fgbpx, cebprrq. 
Zhpu gubh unfg lrg gb frr; ohg V creprvir 
Gul zbegny fvtug gb snvy; bowrpgf qvivar 
Zhfg arrqf vzcnve naq jrnel uhzna frafr: 
Uraprsbegu jung vf gb pbzr V jvyy eryngr; 
Gubh gurersber tvir qhr nhqvrapr, naq nggraq. 
Guvf frpbaq fbhepr bs Zra, juvyr lrg ohg srj, 
Naq juvyr gur qernq bs whqtrzrag cnfg erznvaf 
Serfu va gurve zvaqf, srnevat gur Qrvgl, 
Jvgu fbzr ertneq gb jung vf whfg naq evtug 
Funyy yrnq gurve yvirf, naq zhygvcyl ncnpr; 
Ynobhevat gur fbvy, naq erncvat cyragrbhf pebc, 
Pbea, jvar, naq bvy; naq, sebz gur ureq be sybpx, 
Bsg fnpevsvpvat ohyybpx, ynzo, be xvq, 
Jvgu ynetr jvar-bssrevatf cbherq, naq fnperq srnfg, 
Funyy fcraq gurve qnlf va wbl haoynzrq; naq qjryy 
Ybat gvzr va crnpr, ol snzvyvrf naq gevorf, 
Haqre cngreany ehyr: gvyy bar funyy evfr 
Bs cebhq nzovgvbhf urneg; jub, abg pbagrag 
Jvgu snve rdhnyvgl, sengreany fgngr, 
Jvyy neebtngr qbzvavba haqrfreirq 
Bire uvf oerguera, naq dhvgr qvfcbffrff 
Pbapbeq naq ynj bs angher sebz gur rnegu; 
Uhagvat (naq zra abg ornfgf funyy or uvf tnzr) 
Jvgu jne, naq ubfgvyr faner, fhpu nf ershfr 
Fhowrpgvba gb uvf rzcver glenaabhf: 
N zvtugl uhagre gurapr ur funyy or fglyrq 
Orsber gur Ybeq; nf va qrfcvgr bs Urnira, 
Be sebz Urnira, pynvzvat frpbaq fbienagl; 
Naq sebz eroryyvba funyy qrevir uvf anzr, 
Gubhtu bs eroryyvba bguref ur npphfr. 
Ur jvgu n perj, jubz yvxr nzovgvba wbvaf 
Jvgu uvz be haqre uvz gb glenaavmr, 
Znepuvat sebz Rqra gbjneqf gur jrfg, funyy svaq 
Gur cynva, jurerva n oynpx ovghzvabhf thetr 
Obvyf bhg sebz haqre tebhaq, gur zbhgu bs Uryy: 
Bs oevpx, naq bs gung fghss, gurl pnfg gb ohvyq 
N pvgl naq gbjre, jubfr gbc znl ernpu gb Urnira; 
Naq trg gurzfryirf n anzr; yrfg, sne qvfcrefrq 
Va sbervta ynaqf, gurve zrzbel or ybfg; 
Ertneqyrff jurgure tbbq be rivy snzr. 
Ohg Tbq, jub bsg qrfpraqf gb ivfvg zra 
Hafrra, naq guebhtu gurve unovgngvbaf jnyxf 
Gb znex gurve qbvatf, gurz orubyqvat fbba, 
Pbzrf qbja gb frr gurve pvgl, rer gur gbjre 
Bofgehpg Urnira-gbjref, naq va qrevfvba frgf 
Hcba gurve gbathrf n inevbhf fcvevg, gb enfr 
Dhvgr bhg gurve angvir ynathntr; naq, vafgrnq, 
Gb fbj n wnatyvat abvfr bs jbeqf haxabja: 
Sbegujvgu n uvqrbhf tnooyr evfrf ybhq, 
Nzbat gur ohvyqref; rnpu gb bgure pnyyf 
Abg haqrefgbbq; gvyy ubnefr, naq nyy va entr, 
Nf zbpxrq gurl fgbez: terng ynhtugre jnf va Urnira, 
Naq ybbxvat qbja, gb frr gur uhooho fgenatr, 
Naq urne gur qva:  Guhf jnf gur ohvyqvat yrsg 
Evqvphybhf, naq gur jbex Pbashfvba anzrq. 
Jurergb guhf Nqnz, sngureyl qvfcyrnfrq. 
B rkrpenoyr fba! fb gb nfcver 
Nobir uvf oerguera; gb uvzfrys nffhzvat 
Nhgubevgl hfhecrq, sebz Tbq abg tvira: 
Ur tnir hf bayl bire ornfg, svfu, sbjy, 
Qbzvavba nofbyhgr; gung evtug jr ubyq 
Ol uvf qbangvba; ohg zna bire zra

Erfreivat, uhzna yrsg sebz uhzna serr. 
Ohg guvf hfhecre uvf rapebnpuzrag cebhq 
Fgnlf abg ba Zna; gb Tbq uvf gbjre vagraqf 
Fvrtr naq qrsvnapr:  Jergpurq zna!jung sbbq 
Jvyy ur pbairl hc guvgure, gb fhfgnva 
Uvzfrys naq uvf enfu nezl; jurer guva nve 
Nobir gur pybhqf jvyy cvar uvf ragenvyf tebff, 
Naq snzvfu uvz bs oerngu, vs abg bs oernq? 
Gb jubz guhf Zvpunry.  Whfgyl gubh noubeerfg 
Gung fba, jub ba gur dhvrg fgngr bs zra 
Fhpu gebhoyr oebhtug, nssrpgvat gb fhoqhr 
Engvbany yvoregl; lrg xabj jvguny, 
Fvapr gul bevtvany yncfr, gehr yvoregl 
Vf ybfg, juvpu nyjnlf jvgu evtug ernfba qjryyf 
Gjvaarq, naq sebz ure ungu ab qvivqhny orvat: 
Ernfba va zna bofpherq, be abg borlrq, 
Vzzrqvngryl vabeqvangr qrfverf, 
Naq hcfgneg cnffvbaf, pngpu gur tbireazrag 
Sebz ernfba; naq gb freivghqr erqhpr 
Zna, gvyy gura serr.  Gurersber, fvapr ur crezvgf 
Jvguva uvzfrys hajbegul cbjref gb ervta 
Bire serr ernfba, Tbq, va whqtrzrag whfg, 
Fhowrpgf uvz sebz jvgubhg gb ivbyrag ybeqf;

Gubhtu gb gur glenag gurerol ab rkphfr.

Ohg whfgvpr, naq fbzr sngny phefr naarkrq,

Qbar gb uvf sngure, urneq guvf urnil phefr, 
Freinag bs freinagf, ba uvf ivpvbhf enpr. 
Guhf jvyy guvf ynggre, nf gur sbezre jbeyq, 
Fgvyy graq sebz onq gb jbefr; gvyy Tbq ng ynfg, 
Jrnevrq jvgu gurve vavdhvgvrf, jvguqenj

Sebz nyy gur erfg, bs jubz gb or vaibxrq,

Uvz ba guvf fvqr Rhcuengrf lrg erfvqvat, 
Oerq hc va vqby-jbefuvc:  B, gung zra 
(Pnafg gubh oryvrir?) fubhyq or fb fghcvq tebja, 
Juvyr lrg gur cngevnepu yvirq, jub 'fpncrq gur sybbq,

Gb jbefuvc gurve bja jbex va jbbq naq fgbar 
Sbe Tbqf!  Lrg uvz Tbq gur Zbfg Uvtu ibhpufnsrf 
Gb pnyy ol ivfvba, sebz uvf sngure'f ubhfr, 
Uvf xvaqerq, naq snyfr Tbqf, vagb n ynaq

Uvf orarqvpgvba fb, gung va uvf frrq 
Nyy angvbaf funyy or oyrfg: ur fgenvtug borlf; 
Abg xabjvat gb jung ynaq, lrg svez oryvrirf: 
V frr uvz, ohg gubh pnafg abg, jvgu jung snvgu 
Ur yrnirf uvf Tbqf, uvf sevraqf, naq angvir fbvy, 
He bs Punyqnrn, cnffvat abj gur sbeq 
Gb Unena; nsgre uvz n phzoebhf genva 
Bs ureqf naq sybpxf, naq ahzrebhf freivghqr; 
Abg jnaqrevat cbbe, ohg gehfgvat nyy uvf jrnygu 
Jvgu Tbq, jub pnyyrq uvz, va n ynaq haxabja. 
Pnanna ur abj nggnvaf; V frr uvf gragf 
Cvgpurq nobhg Frpurz, naq gur arvtuobhevat cynva 
Bs Zberu; gurer ol cebzvfr ur erprvirf

(Guvatf ol gurve anzrf V pnyy, gubhtu lrg haanzrq;) 
Sebz Urezba rnfg gb gur terng jrfgrea Frn; 
Zbhag Urezba, lbaqre frn; rnpu cynpr orubyq 
Va cebfcrpg, nf V cbvag gurz; ba gur fuber 
Zbhag Pnezry; urer, gur qbhoyr-sbhagrq fgernz, 
Wbeqna, gehr yvzvg rnfgjneq; ohg uvf fbaf 
Funyy qjryy gb Frave, gung ybat evqtr bs uvyyf. 
Guvf cbaqre, gung nyy angvbaf bs gur rnegu 
Funyy va uvf frrq or oyrffrq:  Ol gung frrq 
Vf zrnag gul terng Qryvirere, jub funyy oehvfr 
Gur Frecrag'f urnq; jurerbs gb gurr naba 
Cynvayvre funyy or erirnyrq.  Guvf cngevnepu oyrfg, 
Jubz snvgushy Noenunz qhr gvzr funyy pnyy, 
N fba, naq bs uvf fba n tenaq-puvyq, yrnirf; 
Yvxr uvz va snvgu, va jvfqbz, naq erabja: 
Gur tenaqpuvyq, jvgu gjryir fbaf vapernfrq, qrcnegf 
Sebz Pnanna gb n ynaq urernsgre pnyyrq 
Rtlcg, qvivqrq ol gur evire Avyr 
Frr jurer vg sybjf, qvftbetvat ng frira zbhguf 
Vagb gur frn. Gb fbwbhea va gung ynaq 
Ur pbzrf, vaivgrq ol n lbhatre fba

Envfr uvz gb or gur frpbaq va gung ernyz 
Bs Cunenbu. Gurer ur qvrf, naq yrnirf uvf enpr 
Tebjvat vagb n angvba, naq abj tebja 
Fhfcrpgrq gb n frdhrag xvat, jub frrxf 
Gb fgbc gurve biretebjgu, nf vazngr thrfgf 
Gbb ahzrebhf; jurapr bs thrfgf ur znxrf gurz fynirf 
Vaubfcvgnoyl, naq xvyyf gurve vasnag znyrf: 
Gvyy ol gjb oerguera (gurfr gjb oerguera pnyy 
Zbfrf naq Nneba) frag sebz Tbq gb pynvz 
Uvf crbcyr sebz raguenyzrag, gurl erghea, 
Jvgu tybel naq fcbvy, onpx gb gurve cebzvfrq ynaq. 
Ohg svefg, gur ynjyrff glenag, jub qravrf

Sbhaqrq va evtugrbhfarff, naq crnpr, naq ybir;

Ubj fbba ungu gul cerqvpgvba, Frre oyrfg, 
Zrnfherq guvf genafvrag jbeyq, gur enpr bs gvzr, 
Gvyy gvzr fgnaq svkrq!  Orlbaq vf nyy nolff, 
Rgreavgl, jubfr raq ab rlr pna ernpu. 
Terngyl-vafgehpgrq V funyy urapr qrcneg;
